Atub

**Atub** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [sorceress](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerIllusionExpert "Skyrim:TrainerIllusionExpert") living in [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur"). She offers expert [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") after completion of [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe") quest.

She wears [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (either [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") or [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish")), and also a [Northwatch captain's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Captain%27s_Key "Skyrim:Northwatch Captain's Key"). She knows the spells [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), [Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Ice Spike"), and [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing").

## Related Quests

- **[The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")**: Help lift the curse placed on the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") by [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

### The Cursed Tribe

After the [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") attacking the stronghold is killed, and if [Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor") survives this attack, Atub and Ugor will argue:

:   **Ugor**: *(addressing you) "Halt! You have no business here, outsider. Leave at once."*
:   **Atub**: *"Ugor, no! This may be the one we need."*
:   **Ugor**: *"We need nothing from outsiders! [Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz") will provide for us."*
:   **Atub**: *"We cannot carry on this way! You know we are doomed if we do not do something!"*
:   **Ugor**: *"Yamarz charged me with keeping outsiders away from Largashbur. You would have me disobey him?"*
:   **Atub**: *"You were charged with keeping us inside the walls. Have faith, Ugor. I only wish the best for our tribe."*
:   **Ugor**: *"Fine, it's your neck."*

When first spoken to:

:   *"Forgive Ugor's harsh words. She is merely doing as she has been told."*

:   **It seems like I shouldn't be here.**
:   *"No, don't go!"* or *"No, don't go! You may not be one of our tribe, but you are an Orc nonetheless!"* (If you are an Orc)

:   **What's going on here?**
:   *"Please, our tribe suffers and we need help.
    Our Chief, Yamarz, was once a strong and proud warrior. Now he is stricken, cursed.
    He is weak, and so our tribe is weak. The giants sense this, and intrude on our territory. Now they assault our very home.
    Yamarz refuses help, but I sense that you may be just what we need."*

:   :   **Deal with your own curses.**
    :   *"We have been on our own for some time now. I fear we will not survive."*

:   :   **What can I do?**
    :   *"Yamarz has demanded we stay inside the walls. We cannot leave. I must petition Malacath for relief. This curse must be lifted. But I cannot travel to Malacath's shrine. The ritual must be done here, and I do not have the materials I need. I beg of you, can you bring me Troll Fat and a Daedra Heart? I have no wish to depend on a stranger, but I have no choice."*

If you refused to help at first:

:   *"You have returned. Will you now aid me in contacting Malacath?"*

You can ask Atub for advice before you have gathered the ingredients:

:   :   **Where do I find a Daedra Heart?**
    :   *"In a Daedra, of course."*

At this point you can also ask her about Malacath:

:   **Who is Malacath?**
:   *"You do not know of Malacath? He is the keeper of oaths, the master of curses."* or *"You are an Orc, but do not know of Malacath, our master and yours?"* (If you are an Orc)
:   *"He is quick to anger, and slow to forgive. One who wrongs Malacath is one who will endure great torment in return. He demands loyalty and strength from his orcs. We have tried to please him, but he is now angry with us, and so we suffer."*

Once you have the ingredients:

:   **Here are the things you asked for.**
:   *"Excellent. Now, you must come with me. You've become a part of this. You must be present for the ritual."*

You will then have to listen to Atub and Yamarz speak:

:   **Atub**: *"It is time, Yamarz."*
:   **Yamarz**: *"You bring an outsider here, and now insist I call on Malacath for help, when he has clearly forsaken me? You try my patience, Atub."*
:   **Atub**: *"Doing nothing will not grant our tribe relief from this curse. We must try."*
:   **Yamarz**: *"Grrr. Fine, let's get this over with."*

If spoken to again:

:   *"I must focus now. This ritual is very important."*

Atub will then begin the ritual to speak to Malacath:

:   **Atub**: *"Now, we begin the ritual... Great Malacath, we beseech you, aid us in our time of need..."*
:   **Yamarz**: *"Why are we bothering with this?"*
:   **Malacath**: *"You pathetic weakling!"*
:   **Yamarz**: *"What's that?"*
:   **Atub**: *"Malacath has heard my pleas! He speaks to us!"*
:   **Malacath**: *"You dare summon me, Yamarz?"*
:   **Yamarz**: *"What? What is this?"*
:   **Malacath**: *"You don't deserve to call yourself an Orc! You're weak, you're small, and you're an embarrassment! You let giants... Giants!... overrun my shrine. Bring me their leader's club as an offering, and I might release you from this curse!"*
:   **Atub**: *"So it will be. Malacath has spoken, Yamarz. Your path is clear."*
:   **Yamarz**: *"Very well. You, outsider, come here! I want a word."*

If spoken to after this:

:   *"Please, help Yamarz. Do whatever you can. Our tribe depends on you."*

Once you return with Shagrol's Warhammer:

:   **I have returned with Shagrol's Hammer.**
:   *"But... What of Yamarz? I see. He did not survive. He... He died well?"*

:   :   **He asked me to kill the giant, then attacked me.**
    :   *"What? Why would he do such a thing?"*

:   :   **He fought bravely, but the giant overwhelmed him.**
    :   *"Ah, that is good to hear, then."*

After this conversation Malacath will speak:

:   **Malacath**: *"Yamarz was a coward and a weakling. His deceitful ways have cost you all greatly."*
:   **Atub**: *"So he has been punished? And what of us? What fate shall we suffer?"*
:   **Malacath**: *"You'll have to prove yourselves, but I'm willing to give you a chance. Gularzob's in charge now. Let's hope he's a better chief. You, place that hammer on the shrine. You're the only one who's proven worthy in all of this..."*

### Unused

Atub has quite a bit of unused dialogue related to (what appears to be) a different start for the quest The Cursed Tribe.

:   **What sort of help do you need?**
:   *"Our chief is weakened. He will not rest, will not sleep. He suffers, and so the tribe suffers. Yamarz is proud, and refuses to see that we need outside help. He needs someone to confide in. If it will not be one of us, perhaps it will be you. Go to him."*

Before speaking to Yamarz, you could also ask Atub more about the curse:

:   **How long has Yamarz been cursed?**
:   *"Almost ever since he became leader of the tribe. He killed Shagrol in combat, which none of us thought possible. But the winner is made Chief. That is how it is done."*

Once you have spoken with Yamarz, you would then return to Atub with his request.

:   **Yamarz told me to go to Malacath.**
:   *"So, he says to petition Malacath for relief? Interesting."*

:   :   **He was just trying to get rid of me.**
    :   *"Perhaps. But he spoke of this "curse" to you, which means it has deeply affected him. It may be worth attempting contact with Malacath after all. Go to Malacath's shrine, southeast of Largashbur. See if perhaps he will aid us after all."*

:   :   **He didn't seem to think it would do any good.**
    :   *"Yes, but he offered it as an idea. Perhaps he hopes it will be helpful, but does not wish to risk personal failure. You should do as he says. Go to Malacath's shrine, northwest of here, and ask for his help. See what happens."*

:   :   **How do I contact Malacath?**
    :   *"His shrine lies northwest of Largashbur. I am unsure that he will listen, but it cannot hurt."*

After this, you would then head to "Malacath's Shrine". It's unknown which location is meant to be the destination here. It's possible that [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave") was still meant to be the location of the shrine, albeit unlikely. Fallowstone Cave lies northeast of Largashbur, while the conflicting directions Atub gives either state that Malacath's Shrine lies "southeast" or "northwest" of the Largashbur.

Attempting to speak to Malacath at his shrine would result in the following dialogue (which is only present in the DialogueViews files, not the Creation Kit). It's also unknown which of these two iterations was meant to be used:

:   *"Who are you? Why do you dare petition the great Malacath?"*

:   **You're going to break if I pick this line.**
:   *"Yamarz sends you to me? The big, strong leader won't come himself? No respect! Grrr... If Yamarz wishes his tribe to be free, he needs to listen with the ears of the wind. You tell his wise woman that, little one. She'll know what to do."*

:   **Yamarz wishes to be free of his curse.**
:   *"Yamarz sent you to me? The great, powerful leader didn't come himself? No respect at all!"*

:   :   **He didn't seem to think you would help at all.**
    :   *"The Orcs may be Malacath's chosen, but Malacath won't help those who don't help themselves!"*

:   :   **He asked that I come in his place.**
    :   *"Yamarz is a fool for sending someone else to do his work!"*

:   **So what should I tell him?**
:   *"If Yamarz wants freedom from his curse, he needs to listen with the ears of the wind. You tell his wise-woman that, little one!"*

After speaking to Malacath, you would then return to Atub with his message:

:   **Yamarz must listen with the ears of the wind.**
:   *"The ears of the wind? Malacath himself said this to you? But what does it... Ah! Yes! I see! A ritual is necessary! This message is for me. I understand now. I have work to do. You, I shall need your help. I need a Daedra's heart, at once! Quickly, quickly!"*

It is unknown how the quest would've differed after this point, as there is no more unused dialogue to be found for Atub, Yamarz, or even Malacath.

### Other Dialogue

When asked for training afterwards, she will reply:

:   *"Your power over others shall be great, like mine."*

## Notes

- If Ugor is killed during the giant attack that will occur on your first visit to Largashbur, Atub can often be found standing on the guard tower next to the entrance gate. See [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe") quest.

## Bugs

- Atub was intended to be an apothecary [merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants"). However, she does not buy or sell any goods. She is part of the relevant factions (`JobApothecaryFaction`; `JobMerchantFaction`) but is mistakenly set as a potential member (rank -1) instead of a full member. Since nothing in the normal game ever increases her rank, she will never be available to barter with through normal means.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=7246)) Once fixed, she is affected by [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader"), but not [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor").
  - This can be corrected by using console commands, `setfactionrank 0005091C 1` and then `setfactionrank 00051596 1`.
- She *also* was incorrectly set to never leave her longhouse and visit her local alchemy shack.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=14178))
- She is incorrectly assigned a Northwatch Captain's Key, which is also found in [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain

## Overview

| Augur of Dunlain (RefID: 00108d7c) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Augur_of_Dunlain "Lore:Augur of Dunlain")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden") | | |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00108d7c | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0002BCE8 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Class Details | [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes | | |
| Voice Type | [Unique](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique "Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction") | | |

The Augur of Dunlain

**The Augur of Dunlain** was formerly a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") mage who lived and worked in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). According to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") and [Colette Marence](/wiki/Skyrim:Colette_Marence "Skyrim:Colette Marence"), he was an upstanding mage and advanced student, especially talented in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"). Tolfdir will tell you, *"He was a brilliant student, an accomplished wizard. Delved into magic in a way none had seen before. But, I think, he became too focused on just how much power he could acquire. That's what led to the accident."* Apparently, it was this acquisition of power that distracted him from magical greatness. A failed magical experiment transformed him into a non-corporeal entity. Now referred to as the Augur, he resides beneath the College in [the Midden Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden#The_Midden_Dark "Skyrim:The Midden") as a glowing ball of energy. He is sought after for advice during [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions"), and during [Restoration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell").

## Related Quests

- **[Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions")**: Find and consult the Augur of Dunlain.
- **[Restoration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell")**: Find the Augur of Dunlain and learn more about [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic.

### Good Intentions

Once you have made it to him in the Midden Dark, the first thing you see is a locked door requiring a key. The Augur will then tell you through the door:

:   *"There is no solace in knowing what is to come."*
:   *"There is no help for you here."*
:   *"Your perseverance will only lead you to disappointment."*.

Remaining there for a few seconds will make him say:

:   *"Still you persist? Very well, you may enter."*

The door will then swing open, and the Augur will be visible. He will greet you by saying:

:   *"Welcome to the Midden."*

Speaking to him will give you only one choice to start the conversation:

:   **So you're the Augur of Dunlain?**
:   *"I am that which you have been seeking. Your efforts are in vain. It has already begun. But those who have sent you have not told you what they seek. What you seek."*

You then have two choices:

:   **I was told to find you.**

    :   *"Indeed. And so you have come looking, though you do not know why. Like others before you, you blindly follow a path to your own destruction. The Thalmor came seeking answers as well, unaware they will be his undoing. Your path now follows his, though you will arrive too late."*

:   **And what is it I'm seeking?**

    :   *"You seek that which all who wield magic seek. Knowledge. You shall find this: Knowledge will corrupt. It will destroy. It will consume. You seek meaning, shelter in Knowledge. You will not find it. The Thalmor sought the same thing, and it shall lead to his end as it has so many others."*

No matter which you choose, the next two options are always the same:

:   **Thalmor? What Thalmor?**

    :   *"The one who calls himself [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano"). He seeks information about the Eye, but what he will find shall be quite different. His path will cross yours in time, but first you must find that which you need."*

:   **I'm not the first to come see you?**

    :   *"No, though you may be the last. The one who calls himself Ancano has sought my knowledge as well, through very different questions. Your path differs from most. You are being guided, pushed towards something. It is a good path, one untraveled by many. It is a path that can save your College. I will tell you what you need to know to follow it further."*

You then have only one choice, with what he says next ending the conversation and causing the Augur to fade away:

:   **What do I need?**
:   *"You, and those aiding you, wish to know more about the Eye of Magnus. You wish to avoid the disaster of which you are not yet aware. To see through Magnus' Eye without being blinded, you require his staff. Events now spiral quickly towards the inevitable center, so you must act with haste. Take this knowledge to your Arch-Mage."*

### Restoration Ritual Spell

The College's Restoration expert, Colette Marence, will also fill you in on him:

:   *"The Augur was a brilliant mage. Truly inspired. Mastered spells others could barely comprehend. He was especially gifted when it came to Restoration. He's... Well, he's very particular about who shares the knowledge. So you'll need his approval first. Go on, go talk to him. I'm sure he's been paying attention, and will be expecting you."*

Upon approaching the Augur, he will greet you with:

:   *"Once again you have come seeking something. The circumstances differ. This time I have what you seek. Are you prepared?"*

You have two dialogue options:

:   **Prepared for what?**

    :   *"Colette has already told you. You must be tested before knowledge can be imparted to you."*

:   **I'm ready for anything.**

    :   *"Arrogance will serve you poorly. Your worth must be determined before knowledge can be bestowed upon you. And so you shall be tested."*

You can only continue with one reply:

:   **So...**
:   *"You will rely on your skill as a mage. Not on your belongings, not on your scrolls and potions. Only what lies within. Survive, and you are worthy. This is the test put before you. Will you accept?"*
:   **What kind of a test is this?**
:   *"Knowledge is power. Knowing spells can be powerful, but applying that knowledge is key. You will be called upon to rely solely on your Restoration spells."*

If you walk away from him and speak to him again, he'll say:

:   *"The trial awaits. Are you now prepared?"'*

Telling him you're ready will have him instruct you:

:   *"Step into the light, and your test begins."*

As you step into the light, all of your non-quest items will be taken from you. The Augur will summon ghosts who will attack you with weapons and Destruction spells. You cannot attack them; your only goal is to keep yourself alive using Restoration spells. If you are still alive by the time the test finishes, the Augur of Dunlain will tell you:

:   *"You are worthy. The knowledge is yours."*

He then returns your items and rewards you with the master Restoration spell Bane of the Undead.

Once you have learned of the Augur, Tolfdir will tell you more about his history:

:   *"Well, I suppose he wouldn't mind... It was all before my time, you understand. I've heard the stories, the same as anyone else. He was a brilliant student, an accomplished wizard. Delved into magic in a way none had seen before. But, I think, he became too focused on just how much power he could acquire. That's what led to the accident. Do you remember what I first told you, about how not being able to control magic could destroy you? I didn't simply mean it could kill you. The Augur's accident is another very real type of a life destroyed. Well, it's been described as an accident. I can't imagine it was intentional. Something must've gone wrong, and he ended up in the state he's in now, fused to the energies that flow through the College. I've never felt it appropriate to ask him about it, about how that must feel. Or, I suppose, if he can feel at all."*

## Notes

- The Augur of Dunlain's toponymic surname points towards [Dunlain Falls](/wiki/Lore:Dunlain_Falls "Lore:Dunlain Falls"), a town near the border between [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock") and [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim").
- Dialogue with the Augur cannot be skipped. Therefore, if you back out of conversation with him, you'll have to start all over again.

# Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing

## Overview

Autumnshade Clearing

**Autumnshade Clearing** is a circular glade inhabited by a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") and its attending [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals").

It is located north of [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate") and southwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone").

## Autumnshade Clearing

There are up to three leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") supporting the leveled [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") in the clearing. Around the area are several plants and fungi that can be harvested, including several patches of [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") and [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"). There are also a few skeletal remains around the clearing. A shallow cave at the west end of the clearing holds the bodies of two [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter"), one of which contains a copy of the [archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Father Of The Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Father_Of_The_Niben "Skyrim:Father Of The Niben")*.

[Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") guards will sometimes refer to "trouble" at the clearing, speculate that it's due to spriggans, and add the location to your map.

## Notes

- The [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill book *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")* can be found to the north of the clearing in a small [unmarked location](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Unmarked_Ruins_and_Monuments "Skyrim:Unmarked Places").
- The [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skill book *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")* can be found in a hunter's tent southeast of the clearing.
- There are several [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") around the camp to the north, east-northeast, east-southeast, south, and west-northwest.
- A total of 18 [canis roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") can be found in the area.
- Autumnshade Clearing also [appears](/wiki/Online:Autumnshade_Clearing "Online:Autumnshade Clearing") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

# Skyrim:Autumnwatch Tower

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Autumnwatch Tower

**Autumnwatch Tower** is a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The location comprises a pair of abandoned towers. A dirt path leads to the southern tower, and a stone path branching to the north leads to the northern tower. There is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") at the base of the southern tower. Stairs lead up toward the northern tower, past an old extinguished campfire, with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack and various items of clutter nearby. There is a non-respawning patch of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") on your right, and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") just to the right outside the entrance to the northern tower.

Inside the northern tower, the bottom floor contains another tanning rack by the entrance, with a set of shelves to the right and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in the middle of the floor. The shelves hold two [deer hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), and a leveled [potion of Fortify Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Potion"). Climbing the spiral stone stairs leads directly to the top floor, where three unowned bedrolls can be found. There is also an [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet") on a crate beside a straw bale. Finally, a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Jornibret's Last Dance](/wiki/Skyrim:Jornibret%27s_Last_Dance "Skyrim:Jornibret's Last Dance")* and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") are on the small crate by a chair.

Inside the southern tower, the bottom floor contains two imp stool fungi, several food sacks and barrels, a loose piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on a wooden block. The second floor holds a bedroll, a random rare [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), two loose pieces of firewood, a medium coin purse, and a wooden bowl holding a [chicken egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") beside a bale of straw; on the other side of the bale is a food barrel with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") on top. The top floor contains a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") that can be looted for a copy of *[Physicalities of Werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Physicalities_of_Werewolves "Skyrim:Physicalities of Werewolves")* beside a crate with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top and the unlocked boss [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). In an open crate beside the skeleton are two bowls of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), and in another open crate on the other side of the chest are two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"). There is a stone bridge crossing the gap to the word wall.

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the towers will be occupied by a group of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). There are two bandits at the bottom of the northern tower, a bandit outside the southern tower, and a bandit chief at the top.

After the dragons' return, the word wall will be guarded by a leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"). The dragon will likely detect you before you ascend the towers, and can sometimes detect the [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead") of [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point") and will fly off to deal with them.

## Notes

- The tower can be reached from Arcwind Point via a wall of dark, sloped rock on the road to Arcwind directly south of the tower. Descending from this point lets you literally get the drop on the Autumnwatch dragon.
- If you fall off the stone bridge to the word wall, there is a small point in the rocks where you may get trapped and be unable to escape. Luckily you can still fast travel from here.
- The dragon at the tower may be killed by undead south of the cliff overlooking the location.
- A [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") is 210 feet southwest of the tower.

## Bugs

- The word may not appear on the wall, leaving you unable to learn the entire Marked for Death shout. There does not appear to be a definite fix for this, though loading from a previous save may cause the word to appear. You will hear the background music/chanting, and the sound that plays when you learn a word will play, but you will not learn the word. The chanting/background music will continue to play every time you visit the site. **?**
  - Killing the dragon and returning to the wall may fix this should the dragon fly off to Arcwind Point.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Autumnwatch_Tower)*]

Aval Atheron

**Aval Atheron** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker") and street vendor in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He is the only one in the Atheron family who owns a business; his brother [Faryl](/wiki/Skyrim:Faryl_Atheron "Skyrim:Faryl Atheron") works for [a local Nord farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolfrida_Brandy-Mug "Skyrim:Bolfrida Brandy-Mug") and his sister [Suvaris](/wiki/Skyrim:Suvaris_Atheron "Skyrim:Suvaris Atheron") works for [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield") at the [Clan Shatter-Shield Office](/wiki/Skyrim:Clan_Shatter-Shield_Office "Skyrim:Clan Shatter-Shield Office"). Aval shares [a house](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") in the Gray Quarter of Windhelm with his siblings.

His day starts with breakfast at his family's residence at 7am. He finishes his meal in an hour and heads toward his stall at the market in the Stone Quarter. At 7pm Aval leaves his workplace and goes to the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub"), there, he will spend the next five hours lounging outside of the cornerclub before heading home at midnight for a night's rest.

Aval wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothing"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223d "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223b "Skyrim:Clothing"). He is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence_Key "Skyrim:Atheron Residence Key") to his family's house, as well as a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Aval's brother Faryl will tell you that Aval sees the fact that his siblings work for Nords as an embarrassment.

## Dialogue

When visited at the market Aval demonstrates a cheerful and a confident attitude.

:   *"Assorted fruits and vegetables, all delicious and affordable!"*
:   *"Come and browse my fine selection! Everything's fresh and delicious!"*
:   *"I've a little of everything for sale, come and see for yourself!"*

You can ask him about where he gets his goods.

:   **Where do you get your goods?**
:   *"Wherever I can find them. If you're the type who worries over where something came from, you may want to move on."*

Aval's normal greetings are just as confident and he will often mix his work and his beliefs in these greetings:

:   *"You need anything, come see me. I'm as resourceful as I am discreet."*
:   *"I have a lot of respect for [Ambarys Rendar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ambarys_Rendar "Skyrim:Ambarys Rendar"), but his views are a little extreme."*
:   *"You look like someone who appreciates nice things."*

When exiting conversation, Aval may either act friendly, saying:

:   *"Take care, friend."*

Otherwise, he will advertise his friend [Revyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri")'s business, but only if he himself isn't working.

:   *"Be sure to stop by [Sadri's Used Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Used_Wares "Skyrim:Sadri's Used Wares") in the Gray Quarter."*

As much as any Dark Elf, Aval despises the Gray Quarter. If asked about living there, he confirms that he does.

:   **You live in the Gray Quarter?**
:   *"I'm a Dark Elf and I live in Windhelm, so yes, I live in the Gray Quarter.
    You must be new around here, or you'd know they don't let my kind live anywhere outside that slum."*

For that same cause he holds a great respect for [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter") who tries to reason with [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") over "the situation" with Dunmer and Argonians.

If the [civil war](/wiki/Lore:Stormcloak_Rebellion "Lore:Stormcloak Rebellion") is won by the [Empire](/wiki/Lore:Empire#Fourth_Empire "Lore:Empire"), Aval will express his joy for Brunwulf's governing and his anticipation of change.

:   **Have things changed much with the Empire in charge?**
:   *"Well, not yet. The Empire hasn't been in charge for that long, and real change takes time.
    Still, having a just and honorable man like Brunwulf in charge can only be an improvement.
    Unlike Ulfric, Brunwulf has shown a great willingness to work with the other races and make us feel more at home here.
    For the first time in a long while, I truly believe that there are brighter days ahead."*

## Conversations

Tova dealing with Aval

As a vendor located at Windhelm's busy marketplace, Aval will often engage in conversations with other residents. In one such conversation he talks with his respected friend [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), whom he offers a discount:

:   **Aval:** *"Friend Brunwulf, how good to see you! If you see anything you like, just let me know and I'll glad offer you a discount."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"That's not necessary. I'll pay the same price as anyone else."*
:   **Aval:** *"But I insist. and with good reason. [Malthyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") told me that you've been speaking to Ulfric about our situation. He said you're going to help us. So few Nords have ever offered to help us, a discount is the least I can do."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"I'm not looking for special treatment, Aval. All I did was talk to Ulfric. For all I know, he's already forgotten the conversation. I wouldn't get your hopes up."*
:   **Aval:** *"Oh, I see. Well, I'm sorry to have troubled you about it. Just... know that your efforts are appreciated."*

In another conversation, [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") will try and sell some items of her deceased daughter:

:   **Tova:** *"I understand you purchase used goods, as well as sell them?"*
:   **Aval:** *"Yes, that's right. Whether or not I'm interested depends on what you've got, of course."*
:   **Tova:** *"I have some things that belonged to my daughter, Friga. She... she won't be needing them any more."*
:   **Aval:** *"Oh, I see. Yes, yes of course I'll take a look. Just bring them by whenever it's convenient for you."*

[Torsten Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Torsten Cruel-Sea") may also approach him to ask about the progress he's made acquiring pitchforks:

:   **Torsten:** *"Did you have any luck tracking own*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *some more pitchforks?"*
:   **Aval:** *"[Revyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") put the word out to his suppliers but with the war on, tools are scarce. Both sides have been snapping them up."*
:   **Torsten:** *"Tell him I'll pay double the normal price. We've been getting by with one broken pitchfork, but it's falling apart."*
:   **Aval:** *"I'll be sure to stress your urgency. It seems like every farmer in Skyrim is short on supplies these days."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Aval's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ~1 | Leveled Jewelry (unenchanted) or [Amulet of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Amulets_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~4 | Leveled [Animal Parts](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Parts "Skyrim:Animal Parts") | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~3 | Leveled [Enchanted Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots") | Best-quality; Max 5 (5@25%) |
| ~3 | Leveled [Ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Ore "Skyrim:Ore")/[Charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") | Max 5 (5@50%) |
| ~8 | Leveled [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 15 (15@50%) |
| ~4 | Leveled [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (empty and full) | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~6 | [Lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") | Max 8 (7@75% + 1@100%) |
| ~11 | Low-level [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") (unenchanted) | Max 15 (15@75%) |
| ~15 | Low-level [Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") (batches of 10) | Max 20 (20@75%) |

| ~4 | [Miscellaneous Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items") (clutter) | Max 5 (5@75%) |

## Notes

- Although Aval is supposedly embarrassed that his siblings work for Nords, his dialogue to you (if you're a Nord) is not derogatory; indeed, he doesn't even mention having a brother and sister.

## Bugs

- If [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") dies, Aval technically becomes owner of [Sadri's Used Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Used_Wares "Skyrim:Sadri's Used Wares"). However, he never takes over running the store; he never enters the store and does not own the store's merchant chest.

  **Mod Notes**: Aval is added to the `WindhelmPawnshopOwnerFaction` but not the `Revyn Sadri Services` faction that would be necessary for him to own the store's merchant chest. He would also need to have a package added to his schedule making him enter the store. However, it's not clear what would then happen to his stall in his marketplace -- and as a result the developers may have chosen to not fully implement him as the backup PawnshopOwner (but then why not just remove the backup alias?)

  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. Idesa Sadri has been tasked with the backup job instead.
- You cannot buy any of the items on display at his stall.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. Aval will now sell and buy the items on display at his stand.
- Despite only having meat on display at his stall, Aval actually deals in miscellaneous goods, similar to pawnbrokers.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, addresses this issue. He will now only sell goods similar to those on display.
- Aval's line about his "fresh fruits and vegetables" makes little sense in accordance with his actual merchandise.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.6, addresses this issue. The line has now been completely blocked from playing.

# Skyrim:Avanchnzel

## Overview

Avanchnzel

**Avanchnzel** is a medium-sized [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"). It contains three zones: *[Avanchnzel](#Avanchnzel)*, *[Avanchnzel Animoncultory](#Avanchnzel_Animoncultory)*, and *[Avanchnzel Boilery](#Avanchnzel_Boilery)*.

Once you start the quest [Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths"), the cave entrance will be revealed on your map.

## Related Quests

- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

### Avanchnzel

As you enter the first room in the cave, you will overhear a conversation among a group of ghosts. This group, consisting of [Breya](/wiki/Skyrim:Breya "Skyrim:Breya"), [Drennen](/wiki/Skyrim:Drennen "Skyrim:Drennen"), [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms"), and [Watches-The-Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots "Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots"), will then move farther into the cave and disappear. There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") to the left of the entrance to the room, on the ledge.

The next room contains a couple [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"), one a worker, the other a leveled non-worker variant. Under the light on the right-hand side, a few steps before a steam pipe, is an iron ore vein. Beyond, you will enter a corridor transitioning to the Dwemer ruin proper. Beyond the first door, you will enter a large multi-level room with moving gears and other mechanical elements. You will see another short flashback of the previous party of adventurers as they gawk at the location before moving forward. While you are walking on a suspended bridge, you can spot at the bottom of this room a number of Dwarven spiders. The bridge forks midway.

To your left, the passage rises up to a closed door, beyond which lies a room with a [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"). The room leads to a T-junction, with paths descending ahead and ascending to the left. One Dwarven spider should be waiting for you at this point, using a table as cover.

The balcony

Following the left-hand corridor up, you will reach the topmost level in the structure. To the left, the path ends at a ledge overlooking the large room from which you came, with a lootable skeleton lying on the edge. To the right, you will find a door blocked by a wooden beam. Remove the beam and open the door to reach the exterior balcony. Outside, there is an apprentice-locked chest down the ramp to the right.

Returning inside to the T-junction and following the corridor downward, you will reach a door barred from the other side, which will serve as the shortcut back to the entrance after clearing the ruin. You must therefore return to the large multi-level room and proceed in the direction opposite the initial entrance. A chest is mounted on the wall to the left of the entrance to the next corridor.

As the corridor you enter snakes around and above some active machinery, watch for surprise attacks from a couple Dwarven spheres. Next, the corridor descends to where you will find a Dwarven spider patrolling in front of an apprentice-locked gate, beyond which you will find a chest. The corridor will descend some more and twist back toward the main room. You will face more Dwarven spiders in this section as well as when you return to the main room, this time at the bottom level.

At the bottom of the main room, you will see two doors: one to the south, the other to the east. The south door has a master-level trap, and leads to a room with two chests and a few random items, including [Dwarven armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armor "Skyrim:Dwarven Armor") or weapons and a potion. The east door opens on a downward slope, where you will see another flashback from the previous party of adventurers. You can find a chest and the remains of a couple Dwarven spheres before reaching the next door, leading to *Avanchnzel Animoncultory*.

### Avanchnzel Animoncultory

The entry corridor leads down to a room with more Dwarven machinery, a Dwarven sphere, and a Dwarven spider. A brief appearance of the previous adventurers (complaining about their lack of lockpicking skills) will point to an adept-locked side gate. Behind the gate you will find a chest, a few iron ingots, and two garnets.

Beyond this gate, you will climb some stairs and continue down a wide corridor, where an apprentice-locked chest can be found in a side alcove to the right. Shortly thereafter, you will descend a set of stairs and find the remnants of an encampment, with a bow and a set of eleven arrows on a stone table to the right of the chamber's entrance. You will be greeted by a flashback of the previous party deciding to camp here due to the unexpected size of the place. All four bedrolls will be marked as owned.

Shortly beyond this point, you will find an apprentice-trapped door to your right, which leads to a side room with a chest, a stone bed, various Dwarven artifacts, and the remains of two Dwarven spiders, as well as the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")*. Past this side room, you will enter a larger room with two sets of shelves holding the remains of three Dwarven spiders (though one is on a higher shelf and is difficult to reach; see [notes](#Notes)) and a Dwarven sphere. On your left, you will find an alchemy lab and one active Dwarven spider. There is a potion and several gems both on and under the table with the alchemy lab.

On the other side of the room, a corridor dives deeper underground, and leads to a door opening to another room with a shelving unit holding more Dwarven items. This room is patrolled by a Dwarven sphere and a couple Dwarven spiders. As you enter the room, you will see an adept-locked door to your right, leading to a side room with more Dwarven clutter, a novice-locked chest, a weapon on a rack, a helmet, and a soul gem. Opposite this side room, an apprentice-locked gate leads to a stone table holding two potions and an unlocked chest.

The next room holds another set of shelves with Dwarven clutter on it. At the bottom of the next corridor, you enter a room with yet another set of shelves, triggering another flashback hinting that not all the sleeping guardians are inactive. Another downward slope and another door lead to a raised balcony running around a large room. The room's lower section features several tables and shelving units holding two inert [Dwarven centurions](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") containing [centurion dynamo cores](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core"), several inactive Dwarven spheres and spiders, and more Dwarven clutter, as well as an unlocked chest on the shelves to the west. Several active spiders also roam the room.

The exit from this room is up a set of stairs in the northwestern corner, leading to a passage where you will find Drennen's body. Traveling a few steps beyond will trigger a new flashback from the previous party of adventurers, explaining how Drennen decided to leave the others. There is also an unlocked chest under a shelving unit, with more Dwarven items on the shelves and an adjacent table. The door ahead leads to *Avanchnzel Boilery*.

### Avanchnzel Boilery

The Boilery zone starts with a downward passage, and a flashback from the remaining three adventurers. In the corridor beyond, you will walk on a floor grate under which is an inaccessible Dwarven spider that can detect you but won't be able to hit you (see [notes](#Notes) and [bugs](#Bugs)). On the other hand, a Dwarven sphere around the corner can certainly attack you. There are two chests and several inert Dwarven spiders on the four sets of shelves nearby. Next, you will reach a room where another flashback takes place, during which Breya says "*Something doesn't feel right about this*". Several [Dwarven metal ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot") lie between a table and a set of shelves, while two potions are on the shelves.

The door beyond opens onto a downward corridor with a [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") trap, triggered by stepping on the pressure plates at the top of the corridor, even if you have the [Light Foot](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Foot "Skyrim:Light Foot") perk. A series of pipes make passage to the sides of the blade difficult, but it is possible to carefully sidestep or run ahead of the blade until you reach the bottom of the corridor, where a lever can be used to deactivate the trap. The body of Watches-The-Roots can be found next to the disarming lever.

The next room contains the [Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon")'s receptacle, your goal for the quest Unfathomable Depths. However, you will first have to deal with one leveled Dwarven centurion that will activate as soon as you are close enough. Another inert centurion can be found lying to the right of the raised center platform. On the steps of the platform, you will find Breya's corpse.

At the top of the stairs is a locked door which requires a key, but which will be automatically unlocked once you place the Lexicon on its receptacle. When you do so, you will also receive the [Ancient Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Knowledge "Skyrim:Ancient Knowledge") ability.

The door at the top of the stairs leads to a room that contains a chest and a lever-activated elevator that will take you to the barred door in the first zone that could not be opened from the other side. Remove the blocking beam, and exit the ruin through the nearby door to the balcony.

## Notes

- You do not need the quest Unfathomable Depths to be active to enter Avanchnzel. The door is glitched, allowing you to slowly pan across the door until a small gap appears, through which you can activate the bar and raise it, allowing you to open the door.
- You can use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to access and loot any Dwarven spider remains found on high shelves in the ruin.
- The Dwarven spider under the grate in the last zone can be destroyed using the spell [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning") or a damage-dealing shout such as [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath"). It is also possible to summon an atronach beneath the grate to deal with the spider.
- Avanchnzel also [appears](/wiki/Online:Avanchnzel "Online:Avanchnzel") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- None of the creatures in the ruin are tagged as a boss, which prevents the location from being marked as cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
  -  To set Avanchnzel as cleared via console, enter `SetLocationCleared 18ee5 1`.
- There is an unmineable gold ore vein just off the path leading to the ruin.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Having a follower wait on the grate above the inaccessible Dwarven spider when it is still alive may cause the follower to somehow drop beneath the grate to attack it. If they do, they will be irretrievable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), selecting the follower (either by clicking on them or using the `prid` command with the follower's [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")), then entering `moveto player`.
- An inactive Dwarven sphere may be seen floating on a shelf and clipping into the one above it ([seen here](https://i.ibb.co/yPWkRYV/Screen-Shot140.png)).
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.6, fixes this bug.
- Just after the inaccessible Dwarven spider and before the flashback scene, there is what appears to be a barred spike-style gate leading into the pipe section where the spider is. This entry is non-functional and cannot be opened. Holding a plate or platter against the gate and using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout will get you through. On the other side are several pipes and possibly two dead automatons depending on your level, but no treasure.
- If you enter the master-trapped double doors at the bottom of the main room in the first zone, the audio for the entire ruin will glitch, either becoming corrupted and crackling or having a long delay between an action and its sound effect (such as using a shout or swinging a weapon). This may also cause the game to freeze, depending on the severity of the glitch. It's best to avoid opening the doors or picking the trap to avoid this bug altogether. **?**
- The second-to-last set of shelves on the right side of the room in the Boilery has a Dwarven spider on the lowest shelf with a tendency to spawn partway in the wall, making a loud clanking sound as it vibrates. **?**

Avanessa Calladius

Avanessa Calladius is a dead woman in [Gromm's Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Gromm%27s_Pass "Skyrim:Gromm's Pass"), the author of [Letter to Clexius](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Clexius "Skyrim:Letter to Clexius").

## Related Quests

- **[Blue in the Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_in_the_Face "Skyrim:Blue in the Face")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"): Investigate rumors of the Blue God's return.

# Skyrim:Aventus Aretino

## Overview

| Aventus Aretino (RefID: 0001B121) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Aventus Aretino performing the ritual of the Black Sacrament

**Aventus Aretino** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") located in the [Aretino Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence "Skyrim:Aretino Residence") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He escaped from [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), where he ended up after his mother, Naalia Aretino, died from sickness during the winter, and he now seeks revenge on the owner of the orphanage, [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind"), for mistreatment of orphans.

Aventus wears red colored [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Shoes"), and is equipped with a simple [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). He carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence_Key "Skyrim:Aretino Residence Key") to his house, a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

Rumor has it that he is attempting to contact the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). If you track him down, you will find him chanting the Black Sacrament and he will assume that you are a member of the Dark Brotherhood. Speaking to him gives the quest [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost"), which leads to your entrance into the Dark Brotherhood.

## Related Quests

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned child avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

### Innocence Lost

He can be found in the Aretino Residence constantly trying to call the Dark Brotherhood. While his actions remain the same, his dialogue rotates between several lines until you reveal yourself:

:   *"Sweet Mother, sweet Mother, send your child unto me, for the sins of the unworthy must be baptized in blood and fear."*
:   *"Please... How long must I do this? I keep praying, Night Mother. Why won't you answer me?"*
:   *"Die, Grelod! Die!"*
:   *"So... very tired..."*
:   *"Grelod, you old crone. You'll get what you deserve. The Dark Brotherhood will see to that..."*

If you attack him he will shout:

:   *"Wait! That's not how this is supposed to work!"*

When you talk to him and ask if he is all right he will be overjoyed and remark:

:   *"It worked! I knew you'd come, I just knew it! I did the Black Sacrament, over and over. With the body and the... the things. And then you came! An assassin from the Dark Brotherhood."*

At this point, there are three choices of interaction, but they all lead to the same path:

:   ***I'm sorry, boy, but I'm not who you think I am.***
:   *"Of course you are! I prayed, and you came, and now you'll accept my contract."*

:   ***Yes, of course... The Black Sacrament...***
:   *"It took so long. So very long. But now that you're here, you can accept my contract."*

:   ***(Remain silent)***
:   *"You don't have to say anything. There's no need. You're here, so I know you'll accept my contract."*

Each path leads to asking about the contract:

:   **Contract?**
:   *"My mother, she... she died. I... I'm all alone now. So they sent me to that terrible orphanage in Riften. Honorhall. The headmistress is an evil, cruel woman. They call her Grelod the Kind. But she's not kind. She's terrible. To all of us. So I ran away, and came home. And performed the Black Sacrament. Now you're here! And you can kill Grelod the Kind!"*

Before you leave, you can talk to Aventus for more information, such as the reward and a bit of his back story:

:   *"Please don't kill [Constance Michel](/wiki/Skyrim:Constance_Michel "Skyrim:Constance Michel"). She really is kind."*

:   **Assassinations don't come cheap, boy.**
:   *"I have a family heirloom you can have. Supposed to be sort of valuable. I hope that's all right."*

:   **Tell me about your mother. What happened?**
:   *"She got sick, last winter, when the snows came. And she just... she never got better. Not all year. One night she fell asleep and... never woke up. So now I'm all alone. And the Jarl said I had to go to Honorhall Orphanage. It's not fair!"*

:   **Are you sure about this, boy? Murdering this woman?**
:   *"I've never been more sure about anything in my entire life. Someone like Grelod doesn't deserve to live one more day. She's a monster."*

If you have already killed the target:

:   **Grelod? As it turns out... I already killed her.**
:   *"You did? Really? This is the best news I've ever gotten! I mean, I knew the Dark Brotherhood was good... just not that good! You killed the old hag before I even asked!"*

When exiting conversation with him before Grelod is killed:

:   *"Please hurry. To be honest, I'm kind of lonely here. As much as I hated getting sent to Honorhall, I really miss my friends there..."*

After killing Grelod:

:   *"Well? Grelod the Kind. Is she... you know?"*
:   **Grelod the Kind is dead.**
:   *"Aha! I knew you could do it! I just knew it! I knew the Dark Brotherhood would save me! Here, just like I promised. This should fetch you a nice price. And thank you. Thank you again."*

## Dialogue

After completing his quest:

:   *"When I grow up, I'm going to be an assassin. That way I can help lots of children, just like you."*
:   *"I'll go back to the Orphanage in a while. I'll give them time to, you know... clean up the mess."* (though he never does - see [below](#Bugs)).

When spoken to in the Orphanage:

:   *"You came to visit! It's so much better here with Grelod gone. Thanks to you."*

If attacked at the Orphanage:

:   *"What are you doing? I thought we were friends!"*

## Notes

- Aventus cannot be [adopted](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption"), even when the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on is installed.
- Aventus is sometimes referred to as an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") in dialogue from other NPCs. Whether this was due to an oversight regarding Aventus' actual race, as he is a Nord, or because he was originally intended to have a more detailed backstory with his father being a Nord, since his mother was an Imperial, remains unknown.
- After Innocence Lost, Aventus will always view you as his savior regardless if you finish [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") or [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!").

## Bugs

- Aventus doesn't travel to the orphanage after the completion of [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost"), as he should.

  **Mod Notes**: The conditions on the AventusAretinoHonorhallSandbox package require that Aventus already be in Honorhall Orphanage in order for it to activate, so it never kicks in.

  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3 created another bug. Although Aventus now returns to Honorhall Orphanage after completion of Innocence Lost with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3, he doesn't sleep there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3 created a third bug. Although Aventus now returns to Honorhall Orphanage after completion of Innocence Lost with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3, he does so too early. He should be delayed until the player has actually left the city, which is when the courier will begin tracking you down to deliver the note.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3 created a fourth bug. Although Aventus now returns to Honorhall Orphanage after completion of Innocence Lost with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3, he can sometimes be found stuck trying to navigate his way to the city because [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") may not yet be cleared when he leaves Windhelm.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.7, fixes this bug.

Avrusa Sarethi

A Crimson Nirnroot

**Avrusa Sarethi** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorApothecary "Skyrim:VendorApothecary") living on [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"). She works throughout the day, tending to her [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") farm and keeping her wayward sister, [Aduri Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aduri_Sarethi "Skyrim:Aduri Sarethi"), in check. She claims to be the only person alive capable of successfully nurturing Nirnroot plants from seeds, thanks to her long-term friend and mentor, [Sinderion](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion"). She used to have a shop in [Vivec City](/wiki/Lore:Vivec_City "Lore:Vivec City"), but had to flee when [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") erupted.

Avrusa wakes up at 6am, after sleeping in any of the three beds in her home, and will have a one hour breakfast with her sister. After that, both sisters will leave to work on the farm. She will usually work in the Nirnroot allotment, while her sister will run around the farm or work in the [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") patch. At around 8am, she will take a quick drink while standing in the field, before working again until sometime between 11pm and midnight. She will then go inside with her sister and sleep before repeating the cycle the next day.

She wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006c1d8 "Skyrim:Clothing") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0003452f "Skyrim:Clothing"). She also carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), but doesn't wear it. Avrusa also carries a [potion recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") on her, a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality at level 20), a few [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Avrusa knows a variety of spells to defend herself. From the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") school, she knows the spell [lightning bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt") and [sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks"). From the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") school, she has access to [oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"). From the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") school, she has [lesser ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward").

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots")**: Go where a [famous alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") could not in order to aid ground-breaking research.
- **[Smooth Jazbay](/wiki/Skyrim:Smooth_Jazbay "Skyrim:Smooth Jazbay")**: Collect 20 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") for Avrusa Sarethi.

## Dialogue

Approaching Avrusa will have her greet you in a number of ways. If you approach her while she isn't currently in her sleep package (which is between midnight and 6am) and you've yet to start the quest [Smooth Jazbay](/wiki/Skyrim:Smooth_Jazbay "Skyrim:Smooth Jazbay") or collect the 20 [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") necessary to complete the quest, she'll greet you by saying:

:   *"I don't suppose you could come back another time? I'm very busy."*
:   *"I have a lot to do around the farm, so make it quick please. What is it you wanted?"*
:   *"I'm a bit busy at the moment, what did you want?"*

Speaking to her while she sleeps:

:   *"I hope this is important... I get little sleep as it is."*
:   *"Ah, you're back."*

After completing Smooth Jazbay, she will welcome your arrival by saying either:

:   *"Always a pleasure. What brings you back?"*
:   *"I'm still busy, but I can always make time to speak with you."*

Speaking to her:

:   **Does your sister cause you a lot of trouble?**
:   *"Aduri is what some would call a free spirit, but around here there is a tremendous amount of work to be done, not to mention dangers that she is not ready to face."*

:   **Are you an alchemist?**
:   *"I used to be. There isn't much time for that in my life anymore I'm afraid. I actually owned a shop in [Vivec City](/wiki/Lore:Vivec_City "Lore:Vivec City") long ago, but I had to leave all that behind when the [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") erupted. Perhaps someday I'll reopen a shop here in Skyrim."*

:   **There's a lot of Nirnroot around here.**
:   *"Actually, I'm growing it if you hadn't noticed. I'm the only person alive that can cultivate nirnroot from a seed to a fully grown plant."*

    :   **How did you accomplish such a feat?**
    :   *"I had quite the mentor. He taught me everything he know*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *about the nirnroot and its strange properties. I haven't seen him in many years. I wonder what became of him..."*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"Back to work."*
:   *"Come visit again sometime."* (After Smooth Jazbay)

After advancing far enough in the quest [A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots") to have been made aware of her and [Sinderion](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion")'s relationship, you will also be able to ask her if it was Sinderion who taught her how to grow nirnroot, to which she responds: *"Yes. He was an absolute genius when it came to the nirnroot. Sinderion made it his life's work, developing all sorts of interesting concoctions."*

### Smooth Jazbay

:   **You seem quite exhausted.**
:   *"Is it that obvious? Sigh. I've got my hands full here. Between the farm chores, cultivating my supply of nirnroot and keeping a tight rein on my sister Aduri, there's little time for rest."*

:   :   **I could help you if you like.**
    :   *"Really? That would be a pleasant change. One of the ingredients I need to cultivate nirnroot are jazbay grapes... the acidic content of the juice is perfect for the soil. I need twenty of them for my current crop."*

:   :   **Sounds terrible. Good luck with that.**
    :   *"I don't need luck, I need rest."*

If you accepted the quest and already have the necessary number of grapes, she will happily accept them from you:

:   *"My goodness, how did you ever come by all of these? No matter, I appreciate your generosity. Let me at least give you something for your efforts... finding all of these couldn't have been easy... or cheap."*

If you return at a later time with the required grapes, she will instead say:

:   *"Fantastic. I was concerned I had asked for too many, but I'm glad to see you proved me wrong. Let me at least give you something for your efforts... finding all of these couldn't have been easy... or cheap."*

### A Return To Your Roots

If you have a crimson nirnroot in your inventory, you can present it to her to see what she thinks of your discovery:

*"Crimson Nirnroot? I'd heard such a strain existed, but never imagined I'd see any in my lifetime. Where did you find this?"*

Revealing that you found it in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") will have her ask that you search for her old mentor, Sinderion, who disappeared in Blackreach sometime ago.

*"Blackreach... why does that sound so familiar? Of course! It's where my mentor, Sinderion said he was going to do his field research. It's been... years I think, but perhaps you could still find him."*

Informing her that you found Sinderion's remains in Blackreach will have her sadly reminisce about Sinderion, while expressing an interest in continuing his research:

*"I knew this day would eventually come. At least poor Sinderion died doing what he loved, his field research. I told the old fool he should take it easy, but he was too stubborn. Perhaps someday I'll continue where he left off, it's the least I can do considering how much he did for me."*

Returning to her with 30 or more crimson nirnroots and offering them to her will have her say:

*"You've gathered quite a few of them I see. I'll search through Sinderion's notes and find some more information about the Crimson Nirnroot and its properties."*

After you hand over the crimson nirnroot, she will go on:

*"Thank you. You've done alchemy a great service by helping to complete Sinderion's work. I'd like to give you this tome...it's one of Sinderion's greatest works. I believe you've more than earned it."*

Asking her about how she met Sinderion will have her say:

*"When I was very young, I was sent to [Skingrad](/wiki/Lore:Skingrad "Lore:Skingrad") in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") to study with him. He was a strange [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf")... paid more attention to his research than his own well-being. He lived in the basement of an inn for goodness sakes!"*

Asking how Sinderion found himself in Skyrim will have her tell you how he arrived on her doorstep one day:

*"Well, after I fled Morrowind during the eruption, I made my way here... my family had purchased this farm and its all we had left. Years later, Sinderion simply showed up at our doorstep asking to stay for a while... said he was going to do field research. He stayed with us for decades... became an uncle of sorts to Aduri."*

Asking her how he came to be in Blackreach will have her tell you about how he left them to do research in Blackreach:

*"One day he simply ran out to me in the field, excited that he'd made some sort of a breakthrough and he was going to head out on another trip. He never returned. From the journal you discovered, I'm sure you know the rest."*

## Conversations

Avrusa and Aduri will often get into arguments. Specifically, they will get into one over Aduri not performing her chores:

**Avrusa**: *"Aduri, how come the fields haven't been tilled like I asked?"*
**Aduri**: *"Because it's boring. The fields are going to do fine... you don't have to dote over them so much."*
**Avrusa**: *"Boring? That food is paying for everything. If we lose even a single crop, we could starve or be forced to beg. I won't have it!"*
**Aduri**: *"All right, I understand. I'll do it tomorrow, okay? Just get off my back."*

They may also argue over Aduri's wish to leave the farm:

**Aduri**: *"Have you decided if I can head up to Solitude yet? I hear it's the best place to meet someone who may be willing to teach me to paint."*
**Avrusa**: *"I'm sorry, Aduri, not this year. Perhaps next year after the harvest, I don't know. There's so much to do."*
**Aduri**: *"It's not going to be next year, nor the year after that! You just care about this farm more than you care about me!"*
**Avrusa**: *"Painting won't put food on the table, but our crops will. Be patient Aduri... it will happen someday, I promise."*

Aduri and Avrusa will converse about the crimson nirnroots occasionally after you complete the quest:

**Aduri**: *"Where did all these pretty red plants come from?"*
**Avrusa**: *"Remember Uncle Sinderion? These are the plants he was searching for... the Crimson Nirnroot."*
**Aduri**: *"They're beautiful. I can see why he wanted to find them."*
**Avrusa**: *"One day, these beautiful plants will make us famous and we can finally move off of this farm... thanks to Sinderion."*

## Notes

- A script note for Aduri and Avrusa's conversation about Aduri asking Avrusa if she can move to the city to become a painter suggests that Avrusa was originally her mother in development, and not her sister.
- Like her sister, Avrusa's skin tone is unique to her and unavailable to you in character creation.

## Bugs

- Avrusa doesn't have the proper voice files if you open the shop dialogue after choosing her as your spouse in the quest [The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")
