Avulstein Gray-Mane

**Avulstein Gray-Mane** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") hiding out in [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). While his brother was reported to have fallen in combat, his family believes Thorald to have been captured by the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") instead, and that the [Battle-Borns](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born "Skyrim:Battle-Born") are aware of this. Fearing for his own safety, Avulstein doesn't leave the house. He's dedicated to find out what happened to his brother, and will ask for your help during the quest [Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action").

The bad blood between the clans has caused Avulstein to never show his face in public so he stays inside the house at all times, either sitting in a chair, sleeping or eating. While optional, Avulstein may leave the house during his [related quest](#Related_Quests) (see [this section](#Missing_in_Action) for full details). He wears a set of [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") with a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots"). He is equipped with a [Skyforge steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Battleaxe"), and carries a [key to the clan's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Key to House Gray-Mane") as well as a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Once you have gained his trust during the related quest, Avulstein will also start to reveal his strong opinions, starting with Whiterun: *"Forget [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") or [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). Whiterun was the crown jewel of Skyrim before... Well, before... Never mind."* and *"This was such a glorious city. But then everything had to change. The Empire came... and my brother was lost..."* He will then move on to Skyrim and its rightful heirs: *"Ah, but Skyrim! Skyrim is supreme among all nations! Our people, our native people, are unmatched in all Tamriel!"* and *"One day the war will end and the true heirs of Skyrim will inherit this great realm."*

He may say goodbye with, *"Remember - don't trust the Imperials. No matter what honeyed lies they tell you."*, *"Best if... you didn't mention to anyone that you saw me here."*, *"Live long. Fight well."*, or *"I've said too much already."*

As part of [Clan Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Gray-Mane"), he is the son of [Eorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane") and [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane"), brother of [Olfina](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane") and [Thorald Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane"), and nephew of [Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane"). The now rivaling families used to be best of friends, but all that changed with the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), where Avulstein's family took the side of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") and the other family chose to side with the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). When asked for a reason on how the two biggest families in Whiterun could clash like that, family patriarch Vignar Gray-Mane will explain: *"Aye, we used to be fast friends, though it was long ago. We were two of the city's oldest an' most-respected clans, an' we could trace our histories all the way back to Ysgramor's companions. But then Olfrid got rich an' decided he an his kin were too good for us simple, backwards Nord folk. When the troubles began, he took the Empire's side. We haven't spoken much since then."* Because of these political beliefs, any friendship between the clans has gone sour, as [Idolaf Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born") will admit: *"Avulstein Gray-Mane and I were best friends as children. If I see that traitor again, I'll throw him in jail myself!"*

## Related Quests

- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

## Missing in Action

Avulstein's presence in the game is mainly tied to [Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action"). Any interaction with him means starting the quest, unless started beforehand. There are two ways to start the quest. Either seek out Avulstein himself or talk to [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane"). This will cause two different paths and two different events:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Enter the House Should you enter House Gray-Mane out of mere curiosity, and get too close to Avulstein, he'll force you into conversation: *"Who are you? What are you doing here? Are you working with the Battle-Borns? Speak now before I put you in the ground!"*  **I don't know what you're talking about.**  *"A likely story. They won't even do their own dirty work now, eh? Well, you won't get the better of me! Now tell me where my brother is!"*  **Calm down. I'm not working for anyone.**  *"No? So you don't know anything about my brother? Then what are you doing here?"*  After he mentions his brother in either of the previous responses, you will have two more options:  **I don't know your brother.**  *"Thorald... Thorald Gray-Mane? Fighting for the Stormcloaks, disappeared and believed dead? You really don't know anything about this, do you?"*  **I didn't mean to alarm you. Why are you so tense?**  *"Because they've got Thorald locked away somewhere, and if they find me here I'll disappear too! I am not going to let that happen!"*  At this point, you will have only one option:  **Sounds like you need some help.**  *"I can't do this all on my own. Are you... are you offering to help me?"* | Meet Fralia Avulstein is pretty defensive when it comes to strangers  The second time you enter Whiterun, you may witness a discussion between Fralia and two members of the rival family, [Idolaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born") and [Olfrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born"). Approach Fralia and hear her tell you about her missing son and agree to follow her to House Gray-Mane. Once inside, Fralia will barely make it through her welcome before Avulstein comes rushing out:  **Fralia**: *"Welcome to our home."*  **Avulstein**: *"Mother, what's the meaning of this? Who have you brought into our home?"*  **Fralia**: *"Avulstein, put that down! He's/She's here to help us find Thorald!"*  **Avulstein**: *"How do we know he's/she's not spying for the Battle-Born? This was foolish! We can't trust anyone! Who knows what they'll do if they find me here."*  **Fralia**: *"I can't take any more of this. No weapons, please. Let's just talk."*  **Avulstein**: *"All right, mother."*  After that, you can ask Fralia for elaboration: *"Thorald's disappearance has been hard on all of us, but Avulstein has taken it badly. He's afraid of being taken as well, so he hasn't left the house. All he talks about is Thorald. Please, help Avulstein if you can. Something has to be done, or we're all going to lose our minds."* |

At that point, he'll force you into conversation as he asks you: *"So, you're here to help?"* Whichever path you've taken, you'll always get the following options:

- **Yes, absolutely. What can I do?**

:   *"I know that Thorald's not dead. I just know it. The Imperials have him, and are keeping him somewhere. But I don't know where. Those damned Battle-Borns... they know something. They're hiding it. They practically taunt us with it. They must have some sort of proof! There's got to be something in that house of theirs. I just know it. I don't dare leave the house myself. So I need your help."*

- **I'm not even sure what's going on.**

:   *"My brother, Thorald. He was fighting for the Stormcloaks, and went missing. Everyone assumes he's dead. But he's not. I just know it. The Imperials captured him, and they're holding him someplace. The Battle-Borns know where. I'd go and search their house for proof, but they want me too. I'd be captured, and then we'll never know what happened to him. So I need someone to find that proof for me."*

At that point, you are free to ask him some questions. If you ask him what proof he needs, he'll explain: *"Anything that confirms that Thorald isn't dead, but is being held captive. I know those Battle-Borns have it. They'd be hiding it, of course. Wouldn't want it to get out that they've been lying this whole time. But you might be able to butter them up enough to lower their guard."* When asked why he think the Battle-Borns are involved he will hatefully respond: *"The Battle-Borns. The Emperor's biggest boot-lickers here in Whiterun. Their connections to the Empire and the Legion are well-known. When Thorald didn't return home, there was no question in my mind. They knew Thorald supported the Stormcloaks, knew he was going to aid them in battle. Made sure he didn't come back. Locked him up someplace to get back at my family. I'm sure of it."*

When you return from the Battle-Born residence with the [evidence](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Missive "Skyrim:Imperial Missive") in hand, Avulstein will greet you with: *"Do you have news? Did you find something?"* When you tell him that you have proof that Thorvald is alive and show him [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius")' request to the Battle-Borns, he will say: *"I knew it! Let me see, please! The Thalmor? By the Nine, it's worse than I thought. So... Northwatch Keep. Then we know where to hit them."* When asked if he is going to attack [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep") he will make another request: *"I'll do anything if it means saving my brother. You'll join us, won't you? Thorald can't be left to those... monsters."*

| Option | Response | | | Result |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Of course I'll join you.** | *"I'll round up what men I can, and meet you outside Northwatch Keep. We'll get in and out as fast as possible. I'll see you there."* | | | Avulstein moves to Northwatch Keep (see [this section](#Avulstein_Joins_You)) |
| **Let me see if I can bring him back on my own. Without bloodshed.** | *"What? You, alone, reasoning with the Thalmor? That's madness, friend. You're serious, aren't you? Very well. I'll give you a chance. But if you can't do it, I will."* | | | Avulstein stays behind (see [this section](#Avulstein_Stays_Hidden)) |
| **You stay hidden. I'll take care of this.** | *"Are you sure? I doubt you stand a chance against the Thalmor. I can have a group of men ready at a moment's notice. Many would be willing to help rescue my brother."* | **I'm sure. I'll bring him back myself.** | *"Very well. I'll give you a chance. But if you can't do it, I will."* | Avulstein stays behind (see [this section](#Avulstein_Stays_Hidden)) |
| **You're right. We should work together.** | *"Exactly. Together we stand more of a chance of making this work. Make your way to Northwatch Keep in Haafingar. I'll meet you near there, and we'll plan our assault."* | Avulstein moves to Northwatch Keep (see [this section](#Avulstein_Joins_You)) |

#### Avulstein Stays Hidden

If you chose to do the rescue mission yourself, a grateful Thorald will ask you why you would risk your life for him, triggering two different options:

**Your brother talked me into it.**
*"I've never known Avulstein to be that convincing! Where is the little scamp?"*

**Your family was concerned for you.**
*"Of course. I should've known. This was all Avulstein's idea, wasn't it? Where is he?"*

You can then follow up with:

**I told him to wait in Whiterun.**
*"A wise decision, but I fear he may not be safe there anymore. They'll go looking for me, and Whiterun will be the first place they search. I cannot stay. Not here, not in Whiterun. It likely won't be safe for Avulstein, either. Our best hope now is to fall in with the ranks of the Stormcloaks. But would you do me a favor? Tell my mother to suffer the winter's cold wind, for it bears aloft next summer's seeds. She'll know what it means."*

Avulstein will disappear from the game at this point.

#### Avulstein Joins You

If you chose to bring Avulstein along with you he will meet you at the lake east of Northwatch Keep with his friends [Geirlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirlund "Skyrim:Geirlund") and [Vidrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Vidrald "Skyrim:Vidrald"). When asked why he is there, Vidrald will explain his loyalty: *"I pledged to aid Avulstein and Thorald a long time ago. There's nothing that could keep me from helping them now."* When you speak to Avulstein he will say, *"We're getting Thorald back, no matter what."* He will then reveal his plan: *"We kill every Thalmor between us and Thorald, and we bring him out alive. Let's go."* He will then follow you all the way through Northwatch Keep and keep his promise, slaying all the Thalmor you encounter.

When you reach the chained Thorald, the two brothers will have a brief conversation:

*"Thorald? Thorald!"*

**Thorald**: *"Unngh... Uhhh..."*
**Avulstein**: *"Thorald? Thorald!"*
**Thorald**: *"Brother? Is... Is that you?"*
**Avulstein**: *"I'm here! I knew I'd find you!"*
**Thorald**: *"What in the world?"*
**Avulstein**: *"There's no time. We've got to get you out of here! Come on, let's go!"*

Once outside, Thorald will thank you and ask why you risked your life for him. Two options are available:

**Your brother talked me into it.**
*"He must have been very convincing."*

**Your family was concerned for you.**
*"Of course. I should've known. Avulstein was behind this, wasn't he?"*

He will then finish the quest with, *"I cannot stay. Not here, not in Whiterun. It likely won't be safe for Avulstein, either. Our best hope now is to fall in with the ranks of the Stormcloaks. But would you do me a favor? Tell my mother to suffer the winter's cold wind, for it bears aloft next summer's seeds. She'll know what it means."* When you return to Fralia, she will be grateful although a bit sad that both her sons had to go into hiding. If you ask her if she's heard from them she will conclude: *"No, nor do I expect to. Would be too dangerous for now. It's enough for me to know that they're out there somewhere, and together again."*

Once you speak to Fralia, Avulstein will disappear from the game.

## Notes

- Avulstein is in the [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") faction and has an unused package to exile him to [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), indicating that he was once intended to serve as Vignar's housecarl instead of his sister [Olfina](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane").

## Bugs

- Avulstein's class is CombatWarrior1H, but his equipment doesn't match.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. His class is now CombatBarbarian to match his equipment selection better.
- Avulstein may be a chosen target for "[Hired Muscle](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Muscle "Skyrim:Hired Muscle")", even though he is supposed to be used exclusively for "Missing in Action".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Awakening

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Find out what the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan") are looking for.** |

Awakening

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran").
2. Travel to [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt") to find out what the vampires are after.
3. Solve the puzzle.
4. Speak to the [Mysterious Woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Woman "Skyrim:Mysterious Woman").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Activating the button

### Dimhollow Crypt

:   *For a more detailed walkthrough of Dimhollow Crypt, see the [place page](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt#Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt").*

After speaking to Isran, make your way across Skyrim to [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt"), which lies high in the mountains east of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). To reach it, head directly east of [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt") until you reach a southbound path up the mountain or alternatively start at the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon") and follow the dirt path that skirts the cliff face east.

As you enter the first room you will overhear two [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") conversing over the body of [Vigilant Tolan](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Tolan "Skyrim:Vigilant Tolan") and two of their kin. Dispose of the vampires and the accompanying [death hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound") and head inside the ruined tower to the southwest, where you will find a pull-chain. This opens the gate near the bodies and allows you to progress further.

Make your way through the ruins, battling vampires and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton")  as you go along. You will eventually arrive in a larger room where a vampire and its death hound are battling some [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). Mop up the survivors and head to the westernmost of the four pull-chain-opened gates in the room. In the next chamber, a vampire is sat high up on a stone ledge and three skeletons will rise up from the water in the middle of the room.

Navigate the honeycomb crypts further beyond, which contain the corpses of a few [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") as well as two very much alive vampires and their death hounds. In the final section of the crypt you will find a vampire fighting a [wounded frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Wounded Frostbite Spider") behind a closed gate. Wait for one to prevail before opening the gate by pulling the lever nearby, dispatching the victor and heading into *[Dimhollow Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt#Dimhollow_Cavern "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt")*.

### Awakening

The puzzle solved

As you enter Dimhollow Cavern you will overhear the vampire [Lokil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lokil "Skyrim:Lokil") interrogating [Vigilant Adalvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Adalvald "Skyrim:Vigilant Adalvald"), who will die before revealing anything to his captor, he leaves [Notes on Dimhollow Crypt, Vol. 3](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_on_Dimhollow_Crypt,_Vol._3 "Skyrim:Notes on Dimhollow Crypt, Vol. 3") near him. After Adalvald dies, Lokil, his thrall, and an accompanying vampire will become hostile towards you as soon as they detect you. Use your starting position on a balcony overlooking the vampires to snipe down at them. You can also close the gate to the balcony behind you by pulling a lever inside, giving you some respite from the fight if needed.

After killing the vampires, make your way to the circular stone structure that dominates this chamber. Pressing the button atop the pedestal in the center will cause a spike to emerge, impaling your hand as a purple light shines up from troughs in the floor. Push each of the movable braziers into or away from the center of the circle so that they touch the end of the purple light within their path, causing the pattern to expand towards the next brazier, until you connect them all. The center of the structure will then ascend to reveal a stone monolith beneath the pedestal, which contains a mysterious woman carrying an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll").

Upon speaking to the woman, she will tell you that her name is [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") and that she is a vampire. She will ask you to take her to her family home, [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"), northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Asking her a few questions will reveal that she is not very trusting of you, but she does reveal that she has been imprisoned for a very long time, since even before the rise of the [First Empire](/wiki/Lore:Alessian_Empire "Lore:Alessian Empire") of Cyrodiil (i.e., about 4,200 years before current events). Once you finish your conversation with her, the quest completes and the [next one](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline") begins.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Awakening**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") (20 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- This quest cannot be started, if you have a bounty more 1000 in The Rift.
  - Pay your bounty before finishing Dawnguard, and this quest should begin like normal.
- Before you head to Dimhollow, [Agmaer](/wiki/Skyrim:Agmaer "Skyrim:Agmaer") will fire steel bolts nonstop, allowing you to retrieve them. Isran will periodically comment on his performance with:
  - *"That's it."*
  - *"You'll get the hang of it.*"
  - *"Take a deep breath and let it out as you fire."*
  - *"Watch the recoil. Takes some getting used to."*
  - *"You need to concentrate, boy. Try it again."*
- You can talk to Vigilant Tolan before he leaves Fort Dawnguard, though you must act quickly.
- Serana will have unique dialogue if you are a vampire. She will assume that her father sent you, and if told that you were sent by the Dawnguard will remark that it doesn't sound like the name of a group of vampires. She will also note that the Dawnguard will eventually figure out what you are and turn on you.
- If you free Serana without killing the other vampires first, she will turn hostile towards them. This can be useful if you're too weak to take them on yourself. Lure the vampires away or use hit-and-run tactics on the pillars, saving often, until Serana is free.
- Once freed, Serana will follow you indefinitely until the quest is completed. Because she is part of a quest, she will not count as a follower. This allows the possibility to use her as a second follower.
- After Vigilant Tolan is found dead in Dimhollow Crypt during this quest, you can tell Isran about it during [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline"). Isran will be irritated with the news, calling Tolan a "fool", claiming that he told him not to go there and that the Vigilants "always had more bravery than sense".
- You can start this quest while bypassing the Dawnguard quest completely. See [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest)#Notes "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)") for details on what needs to be done.

## Bugs

- Upon pressing the button in the center of the room, the initial bit of purple fire will appear, but the quest arrow above the button will not disappear. The columns will move and there will still be vibration and whatnot when it's in the right place, but the purple fire will not respond. When all columns are in place, nothing happens.
- When pressing the button in the center of the room, you may get stuck in a continuous loop of pressing the button. The purple fire does not appear and the columns cannot be moved.
  - This may happen when being attacked while pressing the button. Reload a previous save and make sure you kill everyone first.
- This quest may not start after finishing the [Dawnguard quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)").
  - A possible solution is to enter the console before talking to Isran, and issue the commands `stopquest DLC1NPCMentalModel` followed by `startquest DLC1NPCMentalModel`
- If you have a vampire [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") with you when you activate the button atop the pedestal that impales your hand, the thrall will attack you. The thrall will become friendly again if you sheathe their weapons/spells.
- Sometimes you will be unable to speak to Serana.
  - Saving and reloading the save appears to fix this.
- For unknown reasons, Vigilant Tolan may appear alive in the entrance chamber, watching the vampires while another Vigilant Tolan is dead in front of them. The living Tolan will have the same dialogue he had at Fort Dawnguard, but won't do anything else. **?**
- On rare occasions, Serana will not be in the monolith, and will only appear if you wait. Upon talking to her, she will begin walking away to an unknown location. This may be related to an issue with the [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar#Bugs "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") entrance. **?**
- Having a follower when opening Serana's sarcophagus may lead to a bug preventing [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") from starting. It is advised to make a save before doing so and should the bug occur, dismissing any current followers as well as entering `set playerfollowercount to 0` into the console, then proceeding as normal. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Awakening (DLC1VQ01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've met Isran, the leader of a group of vampire hunters known as the Dawnguard. The vampires that attacked the Hall of the Vigilants may have been after something in a place called Dimhollow Crypt. Isran has asked me to find out what the vampires are looking for. *Objective 30:* Find out what the vampires are seeking |
| 20 |  | *Objective 40:* Speak to the mysterious woman |
| 40 |  | Isran, the leader of a group of vampire hunters known as the Dawnguard, asked me to find out what the vampires were seeking in a place called Dimhollow Crypt. Deep in the crypt, I freed a mysterious young woman named Serana from an ancient sarcophagus. |
| 200 | ☑ | Isran, the leader of a group of vampire hunters known as the Dawnguard, asked me to find out what the vampires were seeking in a place called Dimhollow Crypt. Deep in the crypt, I freed a mysterious young woman named Serana from an ancient sarcophagus. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 12, 15, 17, 18, 19, 30, 999.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQ01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQ01`.

Azadi

Azadi is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") who can be found in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). He begins the quest [Interception](/wiki/Skyrim:Interception "Skyrim:Interception").

## Related Quests

- **[Interception](/wiki/Skyrim:Interception "Skyrim:Interception")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Elite_Armaments "Skyrim:Redguard Elite Armaments"): Aid the Hammerfell resistance.

## Quest-Related Dialogue

When first spoken to you can either brawl him or speak him down:

:   *"Well, look what we have here."*
:   **Looking for a fight?**
:   *"Yes."*

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Alright, which side of your face would you like rearranged? (Brawl)** | *"I'll teach you to talk to me that way!"* | | | | Brawl begins |
| **You don't frighten me. All you're doing is being insufferable. Leave. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Okay, okay. You've talked me into it. Thank you. Here, this is for you."* **Failed**: *"I'll teach you to talk to me that way."* | | | | **Passed**: Gives [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Azadi%27s_Note "Skyrim:Azadi's Note") and warps away **Failed**: Brawl begins |
| **I don't have time for this right now.** | *"I can smell your shame!"* | | | | Nothing |

After defeating him in a brawl:

:   *"You're tougher than you look. You got me, fair and square. Thank you. Here this is for you."*

He will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Azadi%27s_Note "Skyrim:Azadi's Note") and disappear.

## Overview

Azarain

**Azarain** is a [Vigilant of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigil of Stendarr") who has come to [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") to investigate disappearances of his fellow Vigilants in the region. He was staying at the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") but during the related quest you will find his corpse at the [Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins") outside of town, having been murdered by a Daedric cult.

You will need to read his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Azarain%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Azarain's Journal") to progress the quest, which can be found on his body in addition to a full set of [Vigil Veteran armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Veteran_Armor "Skyrim:Vigil Veteran Armor"), a random leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") quality, two random leveled [potions of restore health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potions"), a [potion of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), and one book or recipe (*[Physicalities of Werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Physicalities_of_Werewolves "Skyrim:Physicalities of Werewolves")*, *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*, *[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*, *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*, *[Cure Disease Potion Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes#000f5cb8 "Skyrim:Recipes")*, or *[Resist Poison Potion Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes#000f5cc5 "Skyrim:Recipes")*). A lit [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") can also be found next to his body.

If [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate"), he can cast three spells: [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward"), and [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh").

## Related Quests

- **[Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set"): Investigate the mysterious disappearances of [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").

# Skyrim:Azra's Staffs

## Overview

Neloth is interested in acquiring a staff

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
2. Go to the specified dungeon and retrieve the staff.
3. Return it to Neloth in exchange for a different staff.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Asking [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") if you can aid him in his research may have him make a more personal request. He will explain his fascination with the staffs of [Azra Nightwielder](/wiki/Lore:Azra_Nightwielder "Lore:Azra Nightwielder"), the original Shadowmage, and will reveal that he has located one such staff in a random dungeon. The location is [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"), and can include dungeons both on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Places "Skyrim:Dragonborn Places") and in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)"). Skyrim is far more likely, as there are considerably more potential locations there. Retrieve the staff from the specified dungeon and return it to Neloth. He will reward you with a random generic staff from his own collection.

## List of possible staffs

One of Azra's Staffs

- Azra's Staff of Charming
- Azra's Staff of Daedric Command
- Azra's Staff of Dread Zombies
- Azra's Staff of Expulsion
- Azra's Staff of Fear
- Azra's Staff of Fireballs
- Azra's Staff of Paralysis
- Azra's Staff of Turning
- Azra's Staff of the Storm Atronach
- Azra's Staff of Vanquishment
- Azra's Grand Staff of Repulsion
- Azra's Grand Staff of Turning

## Notes

- The quest can be done multiple times. At lower levels, it is one of the only side quests you will get from Neloth.
- The location of the staff will be a [bandit camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps"), [dragon lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Dragon_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Dragon Lairs"), [dragon priest lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Dragon_Priest_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Dragon Priest Lairs"), [draugr crypt](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Draugr_Crypts "Category:Skyrim-Places-Draugr Crypts"), [Falmer hive](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer_Hives "Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer Hives"), [Forsworn camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Forsworn_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Forsworn Camps"), [hagraven nest](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Hagraven_Nests "Category:Skyrim-Places-Hagraven Nests"), [vampire lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire Lairs"), or [warlock lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"); only locations which have a boss container will be chosen.

## Bugs

- If the dungeon is in Skyrim, the quest marker will point towards the Skyrim map marker in Solstheim. After collecting the staff, the quest marker will **not** be pointing to the Solstheim map marker in Skyrim.
- This quest may also choose dungeons with sections becoming inaccessible if cleared earlier, like [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins").

## Quest Stages

| Azra's Staffs (DLC2TTR7) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | Neloth has asked me to retrieve one of Azra Nightwielder's staffs. It's hidden in <alias=dungeon>. *Objective 100:* Get the staff |
| 200 |  | Neloth has asked me to retrieve one of Azra Nightweilder's staffs. It was hidden in <alias=dungeon>. *Objective 200:* Talk to Neloth |
| 300 | ☑ | Neloth asked me to retrieve one of Azra Nightweilder's staffs from <alias=dungeon>. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR7 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR7`.

# Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| AzurasStarInterior01 | |

Azura's Star Interior

**Azura's Star Interior** is a small alternate dimension within [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star") containing [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen") and any [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") that he summons.

The interior is brightly lit and composed of bluish crystalline structures, with angled ice-like shards thrusting up from the floor and down from above. The floor is made of this same material, forming many hexagonal segments at different heights.

## Related Quests

- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").

## Walkthrough

You are transported inside the Star by either [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura") or [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar"), depending on your choices during [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star"). Regardless of your choice of ally, you will be transported to the same place, and the zone will not change depending on your choice. When you speak to Azura or Nelacar and say that you are ready, they will trap your soul and transport you inside the Star in order to defeat [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen") to cleanse Azura's Star, and in the case of Nelacar, to sever the Star's link to Azura.

When you enter, Malyn will engage you in conversation. He will initially assume his disciples have sent him a fresh soul, but will then realize you are different. Regardless of your response, he will claim to have conquered mortality and run off, saying he's sacrificed too much to surrender now. Follow him down a narrow path, which spirals gradually around and down to a roughly circular area with a central collection of larger shards thrusting upwards. There are a total of three leveled [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") in addition to Malyn for you to face. Once Malyn is defeated, either Azura or Nelacar will speak to you and transport you out of the Star to your previous location. If you wish to loot any [Daedra hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") or other items from the Dremora, you should leave Malyn for last. As Malyn and the Dremora all attack using magic, some form of magical defense is recommended; you may be simultaneously attacked by all three elements. Apart from Malyn and the Dremora, there is nothing else of interest within the Star.

## Notes

- Followers are unable to accompany you inside the Star.
- You are unable to return to this location after Malyn is defeated.
- If you summon a Dremora inside the Star via the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), the summoned Dremora may be a mage instead of a warrior.
- If you manage to raise a Dremora inside the Star and bring it outside, it will never disintegrate after the spell effect ends, and may thus be raised indefinitely.[*verification needed — needs confirming.*]
- Once you kill Malyn Varen you will be pulled out of the Star, so be sure to loot all desired items from him and the other foes as soon as possible.

## Maps

Azura's Star Interior

Azzada Lylvieve

**Azzada Lylvieve** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") living in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") with his wife [Michel](/wiki/Skyrim:Michel_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Michel Lylvieve"), son [Clinton](/wiki/Skyrim:Clinton_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Clinton Lylvieve"), and daughter [Julienne](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve"). He grew up an orphan in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), but was taken in by an old [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") warrior who helped him escape the city. Azzada wandered until he found and fell in love with Michel, with whom he settled down to start a family.

Azzada wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing"), a pair of [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c1 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261bd "Skyrim:Clothing"). In battle, he relies on an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"). He carries [his house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_House_Key "Skyrim:Lylvieve House Key") and a collection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). He wakes up at 6am to cut wood for a long twelve hours, skipping lunch with his family due to an oversight (see [bugs](#Bugs)). He'll hang outside in Dragon Bridge from 6pm to 8pm, after which he'll head home to have dinner with his family for two hours. He'll hang out in his house for the rest of the time, heading to bed at midnight. He will pay you to harvest [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat").

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): The time of prophecy has arrived! Locate [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") for the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").

### Prophet DG

When asked about the [Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus"):

:   **Know anything about a Moth Priest visiting Dragon Bridge?**
:   *"A Moth Priest? I'm sorry, but I don't know anything about that. Try asking one of the guards."*

## Dialogue

His greetings can be:

:   *"Welcome, traveler. Mind yourself in our town."*
:   *"Got a loving wife, a healthy son and a patch of land to call my own. What more could a man ask for?"*
:   *"We aren't a big city like [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") or Markarth, but we like it this way."*
:   *"If it weren't for Michel, I'd probably be dead in a Markarth gutter by now."*
:   *"Seen some mean-spirited folk pass through lately. Thought I was rid of those sorts when I left Markarth."*

When spoken to directly he can be asked questions:

:   **Do you worry about raising a family in these dangerous times?**
:   *"Of course. Every night I pray that we don't get a visit from a dragon, or that two armies don't show up to fight over the bridge. You ask if I'm worried? I'm terrified, if you want to truth of it. But I have to stay strong for my wife and children."*

:   **You mentioned mean folk passing through town?**
:   *"Both the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have sent riders this way, scouting the bridge and the lands nearby. They stayed at the inn, but didn't pay. They said soldiers don't need to pay because they're risking their lives to protect us. And that's not all. They took a heap of our lumber, and one tried to have his way with my daughter. They think they can do whatever they want."*

:   **Did you say you came here from Markarth?**
:   *"I grew up an orphan on the streets of Markarth. I'd have died there, too, but for the kindness of an old warrior named Logrolf the Bent. Logrolf rescued me and gave me enough money to get out of the city. I followed the Karth river north, and came here. When I met Michel, I knew this was where I belonged. I suppose that's it, really."*

## Conversations

He can often be seen conversing with his family:

:   **Michel**: *"Did you read that letter from Markarth yet?"*
:   **Azzada**: *"Yes, just this morning. It was from Logrolf. He wrote to thank us for the food we sent."*
:   **Michel**: *"And how is that old warrior doing these days?"*
:   **Azzada**: *"Not well. He's convinced that his house is haunted, so he's sleeping on the street."*
:   **Michel**: *"Oh dear. I wish there was something we could do to help him."*
:   **Azzada**: *"As do I. That man saved my life. I hope that someone helps him, as he once helped me."*

:   **Clinton**: *"Father, how come [Olda's](/wiki/Skyrim:Olda "Skyrim:Olda") so mean to everyone? She's only ever happy when she's with [Lodvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodvar "Skyrim:Lodvar"), and she's not even married to him!"*
:   **Azzada**: *"That's no business of yours, son. Mind you keep your nose out of it."*
:   **Clinton**: *"Fine."*

## Notes

- Azzada mentions that a man named "Logrolf the Bent" saved him from the streets of Markarth. It is possible that this is [Logrolf the Willful](/wiki/Skyrim:Logrolf_the_Willful "Skyrim:Logrolf the Willful"), especially since he mentions in conversations that Logrolf is still alive and living on the street because he believes his house is haunted, which accords with the fact that in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), Logrolf can be found sharing a room with [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") in [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"). Moreover, the models for the exterior of the [Abandoned House](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_House "Skyrim:Abandoned House") are identified as Logrolf's House.
- Azzada actually has a relationship marker set up between him and [Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag"), one of the smelter workers in Markarth. They're marked as foes, but neither man will ever mention the other.

## Bugs

- Azzada was supposed to have lunch with his family from noon to 2pm, but his work package overrides this.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Azzada doesn't have the required keyword to pay for gourds picked on his farm if you try to sell them.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.

Azzadal

**Azzadal** is the [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") of a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard "Skyrim:Bard") who can be met after jumping from [Bard's Leap Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit"). If the jump is successfully completed, Azzadal will appear and say:

:   *"Been a long time since someone took the leap. Longer still since any survived it. I once performed the entirety of the Poetic Edda from atop Bard's Leap before trying my luck. Well, you can see how that turned out."*

After his dialogue, he will play a song and you will receive two points to your [speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill.

He wears full [Hammerfell garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb"), including an [Alik'r hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Hood "Skyrim:Alik'r Hood") and a pair of [Redguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots"). He carries a [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar").

## Notes

- In [Skyrim - The Adventure Game](/wiki/SkyrimTAG:Skyrim_-_The_Adventure_Game "SkyrimTAG:Skyrim - The Adventure Game")'s card numbered 184 titled "The Reachmen", Azzadal is referenced as being the bard of [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach") during his rule of [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). Madanach agrees to help the [Sheathed Blades](/wiki/Lore:Sheathed_Blades "Lore:Sheathed Blades") in return for helping Azzadal complete his poetic leap from Bard's Leap Summit.

Babette

**Babette** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") with a [youthful](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") appearance, who works as an [assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Assassin_(class) "Skyrim:Assassin (class)") for the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). Despite her appearance, Babette is the oldest member of the [Dark Brotherhood's Falkreath sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"). Babette is the master-level [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), and can sell you many [potions, ingredients, and recipes](#Standard_Merchandise). Like the other Brotherhood members, she offers her [opinions](#Quest-Related_Advice) on your contracts.

Once you have been introduced to the Brotherhood during [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary "Skyrim:Sanctuary"), you can ask the members about themselves, and each other. [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex") tells you to... *"Talk to Babette about potions. She's the creepy little girl - can't miss her."* She is also one of the few NPCs that sells [daedra hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") as a regular product, and often will have one or two in her inventory. When asked for Alchemy training she will say: *"It's as rewarding as it is dangerous. Let's see what I can show you."* She spends all of her time wandering around the Sanctuary, preferably near her [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), occasionally eating, sleeping or relaxing on a chair. After the quest [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate"), she will move to the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary").

She wears [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes#0006D92C "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000E80A8 "Skyrim:Shoes"). She is loyal to all of her fellow assassins in the Brotherhood: [Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn"), [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid"), [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero"), [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex"), [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella"), [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"), and [Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara").

If you approach or come near her, but do not initiate dialogue, she will comment: *"I could brew some potions for you. Or train you in Alchemy."*, *"You looking to buy some potions? Or maybe I could help train you to make your own?"*, *"Brother/Sister."* or *"What do you hope to find? Sweets and my dolly? Or maybe some of my spare Nightshade?"* (if she catches you sneaking near her). As with all Dark Brotherhood members, she will also partake in the radiant conversation system found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Radiant_Conversations "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). Her three unique responses once again show how she uses her appearance to her advantage: *"In truth? It was so easy, I feel a bit guilty. Once again, the sweet, innocent child earned more trust than was wise."*, *"You give me too much credit. For how could I fail? I am, after all, just a little girl. What threat could I possibly pose? He he he he he."* and *"I am the perfect weapon. My innocent, childish form grants me nearly unrestricted access. Poison or a good bite usually takes care of the rest."* When you exit conversation with her, she will bid you farewell with one of the following: *"Have fun!"*, *"Can't wait to hear all about the next person you murder."*, *"Have a good contract."*, *"Until next time, brother/sister."*, *"Kill well. And often."*

While she looks like a ten year old girl, Babette is in fact a three hundred year old vampire. She was bitten as a child and, as a result, retained her childlike appearance. She uses this to her advantage in her contracts; her targets do not perceive her as a threat, and she often plays the part of a scared, lost little girl to gain their trust. One such example is when she remarks that *"I'm just a little girl! The Dark Brotherhood killed my mama and papa, and then they took me captive! Please, please help me! Rather convincing, don't you think? In truth, I'm no more a little girl than you are. I was once, of course. Three hundred years ago. Vampirism tends to keep one remarkably... fresh."* She will comment on her youthful appearance by saying *"Don't let my appearance throw you off. I'm older than you. A lot older. Getting bitten by a vampire when you're ten will do that to a girl. It's been quite a boon, looking like a child. No one ever suspects a thing. My targets make the mistake of not perceiving me as a threat. Last mistake they ever make."* Babette is indifferent about the arrival of Cicero and the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother"), saying: *"Two hundred years ago, I would have lain down my life for the Unholy Matron. But that is an age long since passed. Astrid is my matron now."*

## Related Quests

- **[Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary "Skyrim:Sanctuary")**: Pick up your first contracts as a [Brotherhood member](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Members "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").
- **[The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness")**: Confront the traitor among the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").
- **[Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate")**: Assist [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") members in the fight against the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") assault.
- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.

## Quest-Related Events

### Sanctuary

At the start of the quest [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary "Skyrim:Sanctuary"), Astrid will request that you introduce yourself to your new "family". As you move deeper into the sanctuary to join the other members of the Brotherhood, you will see the rest of the Brotherhood listening to Babette recounting a tale from her latest contract. After she tells her tale, there is some lighthearted banter about each others contracts, highlighting how dysfunctional the little "family" really is:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Arnbjorn**: | *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"* | *"Would the sweetie like a sweetie?"* |
| **Veezara**: | *"Ha ha ha ha! Again! Again! Do the part where he tries to buy you some candy."* |  |
| **Babette**: | *"Okay, okay. Wait. Here we go. "Ooh, you are such a pretty little girl. Would the sweetie like a sweetie? Oh yes, how about some chocolate?" Oh yes, please, kind sir. My mama and papa left me all alone, and I'm so very hungry. I know a shortcut to the candy shop. Through this alley. Oh ya, very good. Very good. My it is dark down here. Oh, but you are so beautiful. Such a lovely smile. Your teeth... your teeth! No! Aggghh!!"* |  |
| **Gabriella**: | *"Oh Babette, but you are so wicked."* |  |
| **Nazir**: | *"What about you, Festus? How did that last contract turn out?"* |  |
| **Arnbjorn**: | *"Oh, yes, please, old man. Regale us with your tales of wizardry..."* |
| **Festus Krex**: | *"Ah, the young and stupid. Always mocking the experienced and brilliant. My contract went very well, I'll have you know. Tried a new spell. Little something I've been working on in my spare time. Came "this" close to turning that priest inside out. Damned messy."* |
| **Gabriella**: | *"And what of your latest, Arnbjorn. Something about a Khajiit? Merchant was it?"* |
| **Babette**: | *"Oh, a big doggy chasing a little kitty! How adorable!"* |
| **Nazir**,  **Festus**,  and **Veezara**: | *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"* |
| **Arnbjorn**: | *"I am not adorable, it was not funny, and he wasn't a merchant. He was a Khajiit monk, a master of the Whispering Fang style. But now he's dead... and I have a new loincloth."* |

After this scene Babette will speak to you once you are close enough to her, *"There you are! Astrid's told me all about you. Heard she pulled the ole' "Choose your victim" gag with you. Ah, I love that one... You're going to love it here. We have a lot of fun, and we look out for each other. Just like any family."*

### The Cure for Madness

At the start of [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness"), the Brotherhood will be gathered round a wounded Veezara. Babette tries to calm Veezara down, to which the wounded Argonian responds favorably. Astrid and the other members then proceed to inform you of what happened, and what needs to be done. Afterwards Babette and Astrid attempt to bolster Veezara's spirit. If you try to talk to Astrid before her first line below, she will say *"You're back. Good. You'll want to hear this."*

*"Just try to relax, Veezara."*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Babette**: | *"Just try to relax, Veezara. Let the elixir do its work. You'll feel better, shortly."* |
| **Veezara**: | *"Achh... Thank you, dear. You are most kind. The jester's cut feels as bad as it looks, I'm afraid."* |
| **Astrid**: | *"Damn it, this never should have happened! We knew better. We knew better, and still we let our guards down. Agh!"* |
| **Festus Krex**: | *"I'll admit, even I'm having a hard time disagreeing with you..."* |
| **Astrid**: | *"Maro is dead, I know. But we've got bigger problems right now!"* |
| **Player**: | *"Gabriella mentioned something about Cicero..."* |
| **Astrid**: | *"The fool went absolutely berserk! He wounded Veezara, tried to kill me, and then he fled. I knew that lunatic couldn't be trusted."* |
| **Festus Krex**: | *"It's true, I'm afraid. Cicero was a little whirlwind, slashing this way and that. It would have been funny, if he weren't trying to murder us all."* |
| **Nazir**: | *"Don't forget the ranting and raving. About the Night Mother, how she was the true leader of the Dark Brotherhood, and Astrid was just a "pretender.""* |
| **Astrid**: | *"Look, we've got to deal with this situation. You've got to deal with this situation."* |
| **Player**: | *"What do you want me to do?"* |
| **Astrid**: | *"I want you to find that miserable little fool and end his life! But first... find my husband. Make sure he's all right. After the attack, Arnbjorn flew into a rage. When Cicero left... Arnbjorn went after him. They disappeared into the wild. Search Cicero's room. Maybe there's something in there that sheds some light on where he might have gone. Let me know the minute you find something. I've got to see to Veezara, and calm everyone down."* |
| **Veezara**: | *"Bested by a fool. Who's the fool now, hmm?"* |
| **Babette**: | *"Hush, Veezara. You were very brave. Astrid may well be dead if not for you."* |
| **Astrid**: | *"She's right. I'll be forever in your debt, dearest brother. Now be quiet. Just... just rest."* |

### Death Incarnate

*"Can you get it open?"*

During [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate"), you are required to seek safety inside the Night Mother's coffin. Once inside the coffin, you will hear explosions and crashes as the sanctuary comes down around you. After they end, you will hear the voices of Nazir and Babette talking as Nazir tries to unearth you. When Nazir opens the coffin, you find yourself in the main room of the sanctuary. The coffin was thrown through the stained glass window, near where it was situated, by an explosion. After you step out of the coffin and talk to the two survivors, the Night Mother will talk to you once again and inform you that Astrid is still alive. She will ask you to find her. Babette and Nazir will follow you after you inform them of what you've just heard.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Babette**: | *"Hurry, Nazir! I'm telling you, he's/she's in there!"* |
| **Nazir**: | *"I'm going... as fast... as I can, you stupid she-devil. I don't see you... helping..."* |
| **Babette**: | *"I'm not exactly built for manual labor. Now come on, you've almost got it."* |
| **Nazir**: | *"One more... pull... Yeeaahh! There."* |
| **Babette**: | *"Can you get it open?"* |
| **Nazir**: | *"I think so. Just hold on a moment."* |
| **Night Mother**: | *"You must speak with Astrid. Here, in the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary."* |

*"By Sithis, what... what happened?"*

After informing Nazir of the Night Mother's words and instructions, Babette and Nazir will follow you until you find Astrid. As you walk around the sanctuary, Babette will alternate between concern for your well-being, *"Nazir told me what happened in Solitude. You poor dear. You've been through so much..."*, and trying to understand what has just happened, *"By Sithis, what... what happened?"*.

After finding Astrid, and discovering her final wish, Babette exclaims her pity, *"Oh, Astrid..."*, before revealing more of her surprise after Astrid dies, *"If I hadn't heard it with my own ears I wouldn't have believed it. How could Astrid have done this to us? Strangely, I feel only pity for her..."*

### Hail Sithis!

During this event [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") starts. As the focus shifts from the dead to the living, and soon-to-be-dead, Nazir tells Babette to pack up. He then takes over the moving of the Brotherhood and the Night Mother coffin to Dawnstar, while instructing you to follow the Night Mother's instructions and head to Whiterun.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Nazir**: | *"Babette, my girl - pack your things. We're moving."* |
| **Babette**: | *"I was hoping you'd say that."* |

[†](#note_A)This dialogue will only be spoken if the quest stage of [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") is at least 2000. However, the highest quest stage is 255, so this dialogue is never activated.

## World Interaction

If you have [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, you may [randomly](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Babette_on_the_Road_Near_a_Body "Skyrim:World Interactions") find Babette on the road near a body between 10pm and 5am after the quest [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"). She will greet you and start a conversation:

:   *"Listener! Fancy seeing you out here."*

    :   **What are you doing?**
    :   *"I am sure Nazir's cooking is great and all, but my appetites are a little more... discerning."*

        :   **You were hunting?**
        :   *"You could call it that. Didn't put up much of a fight but made for a tasty snack. A rich bouquet of flavors, I would definitely recommend it."*

She will move along after the conversation.

If you talk to her again, she will tell you, *"I must head back to the Sanctuary before dawn. I will see you there, Listener."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Babette's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

Babette in the Dawnstar Sanctuary

## Notes

- Though she is an adult according to her dialogue, the game still categorizes her as a child NPC; thus, she can not be harmed. Babette won't be in the sanctuary if you choose to [destroy the Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") during the first meeting with Astrid.
- Babette also [appears](/wiki/Legends:Little_Girl "Legends:Little Girl") in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*, as a card added in *[The Fall of the Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Legends:The_Fall_of_the_Dark_Brotherhood "Legends:The Fall of the Dark Brotherhood")* storyline.
  - For more information on recurring characters, please [see the main article](/wiki/General:Recurring_Characters "General:Recurring Characters").

## Overview

Badnir

**Badnir** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") trying to make a living in [Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine"). He blindly listens to [Thorgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorgar "Skyrim:Thorgar"), and continues to work the mine since Thorgar really needs him.

He will sleep in one of the bed rolls at 8am for 12 hours, after which he will wander the mine, mining the few ore veins, using the cooking pot, or sitting at the table.

He wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") and a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") and carries some [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When spoken to, Badnir will discuss the mine with:

:   *"It's cold in the mine, but Thorgar really needs me, so I stay."*
:   *"Thorgar says we'll find rocks soon, the kind worth gold."*
:   *"I'm the best at breaking up rocks. Thorgar says so."*

## Bugs

- Badnir is not marked as a unique actor despite being named, never respawning, and the other residents of Whistling Mine being marked this way.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3b, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19485))

# Skyrim:Bagrak

## Overview

| Bagrak (RefID: 0005B689) | | | |

| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 108 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 67 |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Blood-Kin of the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin_of_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Blood-Kin of the Orcs"); [GuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardFaction_(makes_an_actor_a_guard) "Skyrim:GuardFaction (makes an actor a guard)"); [OrcGuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:OrcGuardFaction "Skyrim:OrcGuardFaction"); [TownMorKhazgurFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMorKhazgurFaction "Skyrim:TownMorKhazgurFaction"); [Tribal Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribal_Orcs "Skyrim:Tribal Orcs") | | |

Bagrak in Mor Khazgur

**Bagrak** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardOrc1H "Skyrim:GuardOrc1H") living in [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur"). She is the daughter of [Sharamph](/wiki/Skyrim:Sharamph "Skyrim:Sharamph"), and thus the sister of [Chief Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak"). She wears a leveled set of [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Heavy Armor (item)") and wields a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") with [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") and a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), all of which may also be up to [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") in quality. She also carries a pair of [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers"), a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Key to Larak's Longhouse") to [Larak's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse").

## Dialogue

When spoken to she can say:

:   *"You should see my mother, Sharamph, if you need a cure or a poison."*
:   *"[Shuftharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Shuftharz "Skyrim:Shuftharz") can forge you some armor, outlander."*
:   *"Larak is strong, but he has much to prove as chief."*
:   *"[Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath") protect you."*

## Unused Dialogue

Bagrak has unused dialogue tied to a quest she was once meant to give you. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit.

:   **I'd like to join you on the hunt.**
:   *"Follow me. And don't stop until the dominant male is dead."*

This line would've presumably been used if you spoke to her while hunting before your prey was dead:

:   *"Follow me, outlander."*

After you did kill the target, she'd reward you:

:   *"A short hunt, but you did well. Here, on behalf of my late husband."*

If you spoke to her after this before you returned to the stronghold:

:   *"I'll meet you back at the stronghold."*

The line where she mentions her "late husband" is interesting, as it implies Bagrak was possibly married off to another stronghold at some point in the past, as Orcish tribal women generally don't remain in their home strongholds.

## Notes

- The game data lists Bagrak as `InLawGrandchild` of Sharamph and as spouse to Larak, leading to some confusion.

# Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob

## Overview

| Balagog gro-Nolob (RefID: 00038C6F) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Lore:Balagog gro-Nolob")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") | | |
| Race | [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Rogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue "Skyrim:Rogue") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00038C6F | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00038C6E |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 1 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 75 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes, until [Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster") | | |
| Voice Type | [MaleOrc](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleOrc "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleOrc") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionReach](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach "Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach"); [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction"); [NightgateInnFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:NightgateInnFaction "Skyrim:NightgateInnFaction") | | |

Balagog gro-Nolob enjoying a refreshing drink

Balagog on the pier near the inn

**Balagog gro-Nolob** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [rogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue "Skyrim:Rogue") who keeps a hidden identity as the famous chef called the **Gourmet**. Balagog was trained in Breton cuisine during his time in [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), where he befriended [Anton Virane](/wiki/Skyrim:Anton_Virane "Skyrim:Anton Virane"), a fellow student. Balagog went on to publish a cookbook called *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* under the pseudonym "The Gourmet", which became wildly successful throughout Tamriel and led to his being hired as [the Emperor's](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") private chef for his visits to Skyrim. Due to this association with the Emperor, Balagog is eventually marked for death by the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").

He wears [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#00086991 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#00086993 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). Balagog defends himself with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and also carries forty gold, a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots").

Balagog lives in the cellar of the [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), only leaving once a day around noon to fish by the nearby pond. He prefers to interact with other people as little as possible to maintain his secret identity, and is known to most of the Nightgate Inn's regular patrons only as "The Orc". The other patrons pay him little mind, while [the innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadring "Skyrim:Hadring") says that he doesn't care, since Balagog always pays his rent on time. You cannot interact with him until [the related Dark Brotherhood quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster"), in which the only conversation options are to announce to him that his true identity is known or tell him it is time for him to die.

## Related Quests

- **[Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster")**: Assume the identity of the famous Gourmet in an effort to assassinate the Emperor.

### Recipe for Disaster

Should you speak to him:

:   *"Whatever it is, I'm sure I can't be of help. I'm just here on... holiday."*

You have three dialogue options:

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **You've served your last meal... Gourmet.** | *"Gourmet? Why I... Um... Oh dear. You're going to kill me now, aren't you?"* | Cowers behind the barrels of wine |
| **Soon, the Emperor will die. Murdered, by the Gourmet.** | *"What? The Emperor? But I... Oh. Oh, by the gods, no. No, you can't do this. You can't!"* | Cowers behind the barrels of wine |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"Yes, well. Perhaps the proprietor of this establishment can assist you. Please, you're starting to... frighten me."* | Walks away |

If you've chosen the last option, talking to him again will have him tell you:

:   *"Please, just let me be..."*

Upon killing him, you can now retrieve the [Gourmet's writ of passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage") from Balagog's corpse.

## Dialogue

If Balagog is approached before starting the related quest, he will say:

:   *"I can't help you, friend. Talk to Hadring, the innkeeper."*
:   *"I value my privacy. So if you don't mind?"*

All further attempts at conversation will be politely dismissed:

:   *"I really don't mean to be rude, friend, but I'm not feeling particularly sociable..."*

## Notes

- He cannot be [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate"), no matter what the spell magnitude is.
- You may encounter [Balbus](/wiki/Skyrim:Balbus "Skyrim:Balbus") on your [travels](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Finding_the_Gourmet "Skyrim:World Interactions"). He is looking for the Gourmet so he can impress him with his skills.
- One of Balagog's comments when remaining silent has him referring to the location as a village. This seems to be a leftover from when the Nightgate Inn was part of a village known as Heljarchen.
- Even after he is assassinated, the Nightgate Inn residents will still talk about him as if he's still alive.

## Bugs

- [Hadring](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadring "Skyrim:Hadring")'s and [Fultheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim "Skyrim:Fultheim")'s dialogue topics about Balagog no longer make sense after you kill him in Recipe for Disaster.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. A condition check has been added so that the topic is unavailable if Balagog is dead.
- His crime faction is set to [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") even though he only ever appears in [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.11, fixes this bug.
