# Skyrim:Balance of Power

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: *not written*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Put a stop to two bandit gangs wielding strange otherworldly equipment.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad") |
| Location(s): | [Khajiit Caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants#Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Merchants") camp at [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") or [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") |
| Reward: | 300 gold |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE025\_QuestA |
| Added by: | [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order") | | |

Someone has hired bandits to track down items touched by Sheogorath

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad") and read his [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad%27s_Note_on_Bandit_Attacks "Skyrim:Ri'saad's Note on Bandit Attacks").
2. Locate and kill the Saints and the Seducers in their camps near Whiterun. You will then learn the location of their leaders.
3. Track down both [Kinthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinthal "Skyrim:Kinthal") and [Svarig](/wiki/Skyrim:Svarig "Skyrim:Svarig") to their respective camps, kill them, and read their journals to begin the mission [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order").
4. Return to Ri'saad for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

There are a total of four bandit camps to track down

To begin the quest, locate the Khajiit trader [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad"). He and his caravan often travel through Skyrim, but will stop for several days outside major cities such as Whiterun or Markarth. Upon locating him, you will have a new dialogue option to ask about the trouble his caravan has been running into. Wishing to remain discreet, he will give you [a note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad%27s_Note_on_Bandit_Attacks "Skyrim:Ri'saad's Note on Bandit Attacks"), which explains the situation. As the note states, recently his caravan has been beset by strange new bandits at two locations: one near [North Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:North Brittleshin Pass") and another near [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav"). The only other information he can provide is that one group wears gleaming golden armor while the other wears dark armor.

Tracking down the two camps, you will find each location containing 3-4 bandits and a cage. Each group's leader will have a journal indicating the location of the leader of their respective gang, along with a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_Bandit%27s_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Saints Bandit's Cage Key") to the camp's cage. Inside each cage is an [Elytra Nymph](/wiki/Skyrim:Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Elytra Nymph") that you can talk to and obtain as a pet. Obtaining both pets will complete their respective miscellaneous quests. At the first Saints bandit camp, be sure to loot and read the *[Notes on the Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_on_the_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Notes on the Blacksmith")* off the corpse of the [Saints Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Saints Bandit Leader") to begin a quest to unlock [Golden](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden "Skyrim:Golden") and [Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark "Skyrim:Dark") smithing. At the first Seducers bandit camp is a knapsack containing the *[Bandit's Note on Hidden Treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit%27s_Note_on_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Bandit's Note on Hidden Treasure")*; reading it will start the [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter_(quest) "Skyrim:Nerveshatter (quest)") to unlock a [Daedric artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter "Skyrim:Nerveshatter").

Using the information from the bandit leader journals, locate and kill the true gang leaders: [Kinthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinthal "Skyrim:Kinthal") for the Saints and [Svarig](/wiki/Skyrim:Svarig "Skyrim:Svarig") for the Seducers. Be sure to loot the two unique soul gems at the altar where Kinthal is located. Combining the information from both journals will explain that the bandit gangs were funded by a wizard named [Thoron](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron"), and that he seems to be hiding out in the sewers beneath Solitude. Reading either of the leader's journals will start the next quest, [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order"), although you must read both journals to discover Thoron's exact location.

With this information in hand, return to Ri'saad and let him know the two groups are no longer a danger. He will thank you and reward you with 300 gold, thus completing the quest.

## Notes

- The camp near Fort Kastav is next to the soldiers that will aid during [Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav"). They will aid in the fight and start this quest if not already obtained.
- After you've killed Kinthal or Svarig (or both), you may be randomly attacked by bandits from either group, or both at the same time. One of the bandits will have a note from Thoron commanding them to kill you as revenge for their leader's death.
- With [Sunder & Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") also installed, a destroyed caravan loaded with Dwemer artifacts will appear right next to Svarig's camp whether you have started that creation's [main quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost") or not. Reading the [Carriage Driver's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage_Driver%27s_Note "Skyrim:Carriage Driver's Note"), which is found among the wreckage, will start that quest with the first stages skipped.
- This quest can also be triggered when stumbling upon a Seducer's camp by accident.
- If you trigger this quest without speaking to Ri'Saad first, you may have to find him (along the road between Whiterun and Markarth) and speak to him for the quest to complete. In some cases, you must do this in order to be able to continue the next quest, Restoring Order.

## Bugs

- After defeating Svarig, the quest to defeat him will not show as completed.
- After defeating the Saints bandit leader in Whiterun, the objective to defeat them may not be marked as completed.
- After defeating Kinthal, the quest to defeat him will not show as completed.
- After reading both journals, the next quest, Restoring Order, does not appear.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_QuestA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_QuestA`.

# Skyrim:Balbus

## Overview

| Balbus | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | Radiant | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | Radiant (1-25) | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000B5D42 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 35-489 | | |

| Voice Type | [MaleYoungEager](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleYoungEager "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleYoungEager") | | |

Balbus

**Balbus** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who can be [encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Finding_the_Gourmet "Skyrim:World Interactions") wandering randomly around Skyrim, gathering [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") for [the Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob").

He wears some farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#00017695 "Skyrim:Clothes"), along with a pair of [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers") and a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He carries a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*, [his fork](/wiki/Skyrim:Balbus%27s_Fork "Skyrim:Balbus's Fork"), some [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), as well as the ingredients he is supposed to give you. He wields a [leveled dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") in combat.

## Dialogue

Balbus will occasionally comment:

:   *"You know, I've heard the Gourmet is in Skyrim right now."*

When you initiate conversation with him for the first time, you may greet him, and he'll explain what he's doing:

:   *"I'm collecting ingredients to bring to the Gourmet. He'll think my tastes so refined when I offer them to him. You have heard of the Gourmet?"*

You will now have three dialogue choices, the first two are always available, but the third option is only available if you have completed [Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster") and possess the [Gourmet's Writ of Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage").

:   **"I have."**
:   *"Then you know that that Gourmet*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *keeps his identity a secret. I'm hoping to discover who he is, so I can tell him how he changed my life. For all I know, the Gourmet is a woman!"*
:   **"Never heard of him."**
:   *"You've not heard of the Gourmet? Author of "[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")"? He's a wizard with a spatula. Well, not an actual wizard, but his recipes are legendary."*
:   **"I am the Gourmet!" (Show Writ of Passage)**
:   *"Oh my! You? It is an honor! Your food has opened my eyes to the wonders this world can hold. I've cooked every dish in your book, and I must say your brilliance is inspiring. My technique doesn't even approach yours...but whose would?"*

The third option will cause Balbus to continue:

:   *"Allow me to give you this, the fork I used the first time I tasted one of your dishes. Oh, and these ingredients I've been collecting for you. I've risked life and limb so that you may create another masterpiece. Make sure to think of me when you use them!"*

He will give you his fork, a [daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart"), a [spider egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), and some [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat").

If the third option has been selected, when leaving him, he may say:

:   *"I can't believe I just met the Gourmet!"*

## Notes

- After your first encounter with him, Balbus may stay where he is for the rest of your game. As this position will normally be a typical location for [random encounters](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions"), he may be killed if you trigger another encounter at that spot.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. He will now unload properly after you leave the area.
  - PC users can prevent his death by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to set his [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") flag, so random creatures can't kill him.
- The random encounter with Balbus may still not shut down due to the alias not registering itself to stop the scene when Balbus unloads.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. In addition to fixing this, the scene will no longer run if he has given you the Gourmet reward, or if he has been killed at some point.
- He has both of the ingredients needed for [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe").

# Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper's House

## Overview

Baldor Iron-Shaper's House

**Baldor Iron-Shaper's House** is the home of [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

It is on the south side of the village, between [Deor Woodcutter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter%27s_House "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter's House") to the west and the [Shaman's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Shaman%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Shaman's Hut") to the east.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") |

### Exterior

The building has two entrances, both on the north side, with one to the east and one to the west. To the east is a complete blacksmithing area, complete with a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelting "Skyrim:Smelting"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), with an open box on a crate between the tanning rack and workbench containing two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). Between the two entrances is another tanning rack, a fish barrel, a crate with a [snow fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Fox Pelt") on top, and another workbench. To the right of the west entrance is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush. The east entrance is unlocked, and the west entrance has a novice lock.

### Baldor Iron-Shaper's House

The entrance leads into a large room with a large mezzanine above. On your left is a small round table and two chair. On the table is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). Against the south wall is the flight of stairs to the top floor and under the stairs is a barrel and four sacks. In the southwest corner of the room is a small square table and two chairs, a bottle of wine, a bowl of [horker stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Stew "Skyrim:Horker Stew") and a plate with a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") are on the table. Above the table is a large hanging rack with three [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids hanging from it. There is a wall shelf by the table on the west wall with a shield plaque holding a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") and two crossed [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"). To the right of this are two wall shelves with a sack on and a wood pile and [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") underneath. Beside this is a bucket containing with quivers of [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") and then a fireplace. There is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") in front of the fireplace and a shelf above with a bottle of wine on it. There is a stool to the right of the fire. There is a crate with an long open crate to the right inside the crate are six pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), three pieces of [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") and a piece of [malachite ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore"). Above these is a wall shelf containing a [blacksmith's potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Potion"), a bottle of wine and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and beside the crate is a small open crate containing nine [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"). The room continues into a small bedroom area along the west wall. In the small bedroom area is a single bed along the northern wall with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") and a copy of *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v2 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2")*.

To the right of the entrance is a cupboard, on it's shelves are two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") and [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). To the left is a fish barrel with a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") on top and a sack on the floor beside it. Around the corner against the east wall is a pair of weapon racks separated by an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"). The weapon rack on the right has a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and the one on the left has an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"). Next to this is an open crate with five iron and four [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"). Around the corner again is a small round table and chair with a bottle of ale on the table. To the left of this is a second entrance. To the left of this entrance is a dresser with a [fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Fox Pelt") and [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt") on top and in the northeast corner is a bucket with three pieces of large [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"). Against the north wall is a second flight of stairs up to the top floor. Under these stairs are two barrels-one of which has four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") on, a crate, four sacks and a dresser. There is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on top of the dresser. Between this and the small bedroom area is a weapon rack holding a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe").

Climbing the stairs by the south wall there is a barrel and sack at the top. Following the floor to the north you pass a narrow table on your right with a copy of *[Forge, Hammer and Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge,_Hammer_and_Anvil "Skyrim:Forge, Hammer and Anvil")* and an eidar cheese wedge. Opposite this is an open crate with two iron ore pieces and three [iron daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Next to this are two crates with a leather strip and [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on top. On the right is the main mezzanine area with a crate with an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and a leather strip on. To the left of this is an open crate with a leather strip and two more large pieces of charcoal. Against the west wall is a low table with a display case on containing two iron daggers with a chair to the right of it. At the end by the stairs up from downstairs is a cupboard, on the shelves is a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes"), a steel ingot and two iron.

Baldor Iron-Shaper

**Baldor Iron-Shaper** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") living in [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper%27s_House "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper's House") at [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). He is initially found at the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone") before going missing from the village, where he can be found at an [abandoned lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Lodge "Skyrim:Abandoned Lodge") during the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim").

He wears a [Skaal coat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Boots "Skyrim:Skaal Boots") and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Gloves "Skyrim:Skaal Gloves"), and he carries a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Baldor's House Key") to his house, and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**: Find a blacksmith missing from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

### A New Source of Stalhrim

Baldor Iron-Shaper in the Abandoned Lodge

When you enter the lodge you can hear him shouting:

:   *"Please, someone, help me!"*
:   *"Help! Somebody!"*
:   *"I have been taken against my will! I am in need of rescue!"*

When spoken to directly:

:   *"Outsider! I remember you. You're the one who freed the Skaal from the dark spell. Thank the All-Maker that you have come. These accursed elves have taken me from my home."*
:   **Are you hurt badly? Do you need healing?**
:   *"No, no, my wounds are not serious. I don't think the elves were trying to harm me. Perhaps they intended to frighten me. At worst, I have a few bruises to show for my ordeal."*
:   **Why would the Thalmor abduct you?**
:   *"I do not know this word Thalmor, but if you mean the elves, they were trying to learn the secrets of forging Stalhrim. Their leader, an elf named Ancarion, has a map. He says that it shows the location of a hidden source of Stalhrim."*
:   **Stalhrim? What's that?**
:   *"Enchanted ice as hard as iron and cold as death. Stalhrim can be forged into deadly weapons, but the art is known only to the smiths of the Skaal."*
:   **Where can I find this Ancarion?**
:   *"They have a ship. They took me there and showed me the map. You will find it on the northern coast of the island. Please, do not let Ancarion make his weapons. Kill him or let him live, but take the map from him. It belongs with the Skaal. I will return to the village. When you have the map, please bring it to me there. And thank you. May the All-Maker bless your days."*

If spoken to while he is walking back to the village:

:   *"I can't speak now, friend. I must return home."*

Once you return with the map:

:   *"It is good to see you again, my friend. Did you find the elves at their ship?"*
:   **Yes, and I've brought you the map to the Stalhrim source.**
:   *"I know you faced great danger to bring this map to me. There are no words to tell how glad my heart is. Thank you. I name you friend of the Skaal, and I will trust you with the knowledge of forging Stalhrim. If you bring Stalhrim here to my forge, you can use my tools to make what you will from it. Until our next meeting, Skaal-friend, may your hunts always bring you game and your crops grow tall and bountiful."*

### The Gardener of Men

Baldor will witness [Storn](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider")'s death during the quest, exclaiming:

:   *"By the All-Maker!"*

He will approach the corpse afterwards to pay his respects.

:   **Baldor Iron-Shaper:** *"I... uh... you'll be missed, old man."*

If you speak to him, he'll say:

:   *"He was a good man. The strong center of the Skaal. If you know how to stop whatever that was, go and stop it."*
:   *"Terrible times."*

## Dialogue

After freeing the Wind Stone from Miraak's control, he'll say:

:   *"I... I don't know how I got here."*
:   *"Is this a dream? No, it is a nightmare, surely."*

He has several greetings back in Skaal Village:

:   *"I fear to think what would have happened if you hadn't saved me from the elves."*
:   *"The weapons of the Skaal will never be dull as long as Baldor Iron-Shaper tends the forge."*
:   *"There have been many strangers in our lands these past few moons."*
:   *"We call you a friend, but you must still respect our ways."*
:   *"The Dark Elves sometimes visit our village, though it's been awhile since I've seen one."*

He can be asked questions:

:   **Tell me about forging Stalhlrim.**
:   *"Well, first you'll need to obtain some Stalhrim, of course, and then you'll need to work it."*

:   :   **Where can I obtain Stalhrim?**
    :   *"You can find some in Raven Rock Mine, as well as that new source of Stalhrim on the map you recovered from the elves. Just be sure to bring an ancient Nord pickaxe with you. It's the only pickaxe that can mine the Stalhrim properly without breaking it."*

:   :   **Once I've got Stalhrim, how do I forge it into something useful?**
    :   *"With skill and patience. It's very much like working ebony. Yes... I'd say if you know how to forge ebony, then you know everything you need to know in order to forge Stalhrim."*

When exiting conversation:

:   *"Strong steel guard you, friend."*
:   *"Farewell, strong one."*

### Conversations

Baldor may have some random conversations with his apprentice Morwen:

:   **Baldor**: *"We're nearly out of coal again."*
:   **Morwen**: *"I could travel to Raven Rock and purchase some more."*
:   **Baldor**: *"True, but I think that Edla would be hurt if you didn't give her the chance to trade for it first."*
:   **Baldor**: *"You know how happy it makes her to play the village peddler."*
:   **Morwen**: *"You speak the truth, Baldor. It makes my heart glad to see her keeping busy after Heifnir's death."*
:   **Morwen**: *"Very well, I'll ask Edla to trade for some coal."*

:   **Morwen**: *"Why have you never taken a wife, Baldor?"*
:   **Baldor**: *"Because I already have a wife, and I wouldn't want to make her jealous."*
:   **Morwen**: *"Oh? And what is her name, this secret wife of yours?"*
:   **Baldor**: *"Her name is forge. Now be silent before she hears you and becomes angry."*

:   **Morwen**: *"It's tradition that the son of the smith takes his father's place, but you have no son. Who will become smith of the Skaal after you."*
:   **Baldor**: *"All-Maker willing, young Nikulas will take an interest. I would be happy to teach him."*
:   **Morwen**: *"Nikulas is restless. He's like an eagle, always seeking to fly somewhere new."*
:   **Morwen**: *"I do not think he has the patience to work the forge."*
:   **Baldor**: *"Well, Deor and Yrsa are still young. In time, I'm sure that they will have many children."*
:   **Baldor**: *"Perhaps one of them will want to learn the ways of iron-shaping."*

## Notes

- While Baldor is a blacksmith and is in appropriate merchant and citizen/resident factions, he has a combat class (CNAM) record of `EncClassDremoraMelee` or "Dremora".

## Bugs

- Baldor is incorrectly configured to buy any type of item by default even though being a blacksmith is supposed to restrict him to weapons, armor, and smithing equipment.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.8, addresses this issue. You now need to have the Merchant perk active to sell him anything else.
