_06.jpg)

Snapleg Cave

These **bandits** are all male [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)").

They wear leveled [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); up to level 6 they will wear [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") or [banded iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor"), and [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). Up to level 18 they wear [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), and [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots") or [steel shin boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shin_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Shin Boots"). From level 18 onward, they wear [steel plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor") and [steel plate boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Plate Boots"). Additionally, there is a 50% chance they will wear gauntlets and/or a helmet, also leveled; up to level 6 they can be [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") and/or an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"). Up to level 18, there are two variations of each item, specifically [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets") or [steel imperial gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Imperial_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Imperial Gauntlets") for the hands, and a [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet") or a [steel horned helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Horned_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Horned Helmet"). From level 18 onward, they can wear [steel plate gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Plate Gauntlets") and/or a [steel plate helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Plate Helmet").

Their weapon is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). They always carry three [health potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and some random loot. They also have a slim chance of carrying a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- [Snapleg Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Snapleg_Cave "Skyrim:Snapleg Cave"), just before a chest in the same chamber as a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider").
- Within the third chamber of [Haemar's Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame#Haemar.27s_Cavern "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame"), just before the ramp leading further down into [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame#Haemar.27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame") and next to another dead bandit.
- [Duskglow Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Duskglow_Crevice "Skyrim:Duskglow Crevice"), in front of a small fire with a leveled [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") nearby.
- Upstairs portion of Duskglow Crevice where the cave becomes more of a Nordic ruin.
- Within the second corridor, past the first chamber upon entering [Volskygge](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge "Skyrim:Volskygge").
- In [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair"), on the upper level, east of the huge central chamber.
- To the right upon entering the [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") ruins.
- Outside of Ustengrav, near the campsite. This bandit may also be [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie") by a nearby leveled [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-23353&y=89699)
- Just outside of [Roadside Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins") along with another dead bandit. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-43332&y=-78933)
- Inside of a cage hanging over the entrance into [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor")'s courtyard area. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-12986&y=-10122)

_08.jpg)

Haemar's Shame

These **bandits** are all female [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)").

They wear a randomly determined set of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is always a 50% chance they will wear [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ for both shoes and armor; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [studded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor"), at level 6-18, it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally, they have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19, it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of them carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Their weapon is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). They always carry three potions, some random loot, and a bit of gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- One inside [Fort Snowhawk Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk_Prison "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk Prison"), in a cage.
- In a cart situated within a corridor of [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep").
- Within the third chamber of [Haemar's Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame#Haemar.27s_Cavern "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame"), just before the ramp leading further down into [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame").
- In [Bleakcoast Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakcoast_Cave "Skyrim:Bleakcoast Cave"), in a room off the western wall of the main chamber, near a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") and the dead body of a [novice conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Conjurer "Skyrim:Novice Conjurer").
- In [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair"), the first huge chamber, near the copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*.
- In [Volskygge Passages](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge#Volskygge_Passages "Skyrim:Volskygge"), directly below a lever opening a secret passage nearby.
- In [Greywater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Greywater_Grotto "Skyrim:Greywater Grotto"), at the base of the first huge waterfall.
- On top of a barrel near the open pit fire in [Graywinter Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Graywinter_Watch "Skyrim:Graywinter Watch").
- In [Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel"), within the first main chamber, alongside another dead bandit.
- [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock"), underneath the fallen tree acting as a bridge overhead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=37244&y=-69186)
- In a small alcove slightly northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") and southeast of [Shor's Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Watchtower "Skyrim:Shor's Watchtower"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=175426&y=-56771)
- Within a broken tower near [Dragontooth Crater](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragontooth_Crater "Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-141261&y=52135)
- In a small alcove slightly south of [Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave") with a [cave bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear "Skyrim:Cave Bear") nearby. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-113530&y=88011)

_09.jpg)

Ustengrav

These **bandits** are all male [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)").

They wear randomly determined [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is a 50% chance it will be [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally,they have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of them carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Their weapon of choice is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). They also carry a bit of random loot, food and drink, with a slim chance of a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- One inside [Fort Snowhawk Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk_Prison "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk Prison"), in a cell.
- Another inside [Fort Snowhawk Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk_Prison "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk Prison"), in the secret passageway.
- In the first chamber of [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair"), on the floor.
- In Silverdrift Lair, in front of the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall").
- [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat") in the center of the dining area.
- In [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav"), right after entering.
- In Ustengrav, in the eastern part of the first chamber.
- In [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt"), in the southeastern corner, near an open cage.
- In the central chamber of [Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass").
- On top of a rock near an open fire pit in [Graywinter Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Graywinter_Watch "Skyrim:Graywinter Watch").
- In the second chamber of [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave"), alongside two other dead bandits in a small alcove.
- Just past the first cages in [Ravenscar Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hollow "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow"), near another dead bandit and a dead [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan").
- Within an adept-locked cage in Ravenscar Hollow, near two [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").
- In the center of the wolf arena in the [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"), along with two other dead bandits.
- In [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)"), in the first chamber, near a dead [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever").
- In Bleak Falls Barrow, on the steps leading to a sarcophagus, near the first bandit camp.
- In [Darkshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkshade "Skyrim:Darkshade"), in the northwestern corner of the huge northern chamber.
- In the main chamber of [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout#Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"), located within the stream.
- Four can be found within [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast"); three can be found within a partially submerged cage, another can be found inside of a cage alongside a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe"), while the last can be found in a room in the upper portion of the ruin itself.
- Inside [Korvanjund](/wiki/Skyrim:Korvanjund "Skyrim:Korvanjund"), in the very first chamber, near a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit"). [[¹]](#intnote_civilwar)
- Outside Korvanjund, just near the entrance. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=55838&y=32183) [[¹]](#intnote_civilwar)
- Outside Korvanjund, lying on the steps leading to the entrance. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=55206&y=33666) [[¹]](#intnote_civilwar)
- Outside Korvanjund, on a ledge a few feet north of the entrance. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=55609&y=32822) [[¹]](#intnote_civilwar)
- On the road north of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"), near a cart with a chest and three hostile bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-84380&y=25210)
- Near the entrance into [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-23038&y=87936)
- Just outside of [Roadside Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins") along with another dead bandit. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-43261&y=-79120)

[^¹](#note_tg)These bodies are only enabled during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown").

## Orc Male

| Bandit | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000328D7 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

_10.jpg)

Mzinchaleft Depths

These **bandits** are all male [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)").

They wear a randomly determined set of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is always a 50% chance they will wear a pair of [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ for both shoes and armor; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). They also carry a leveled light [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor#Shield "Skyrim:Light Armor"), up to elven quality at level 15 and have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled bracers, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers").

Their weapon is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). They carry a bit of random loot, food and drink, and some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- One can be found inside [Fort Snowhawk Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk_Prison "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk Prison"), on a bloodstained table.
- One can be found inside of [Mzinchaleft Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft_Depths "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft Depths"), within a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") tent.
- In a small room within [Lost Echo Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Echo_Cave "Skyrim:Lost Echo Cave"), alongside a dead [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)").
- Within the third chamber of [Haemar's Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame#Haemar.27s_Cavern "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame"), just before the ramp leading further down into [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame#Haemar.27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame") and next to another dead bandit.
- Three can be found inside [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair"); one in the first huge chamber, near a bonfire, the second can be found southeast of the huge chamber, on a bedroll, and the third can be found in front of the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall").
- In the first room of [Irkngthand Arcanex](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand#Irkngthand_Arcanex "Skyrim:Irkngthand"), on a flight of stairs.[[¹]](#intnote_tg)
- In the second chamber of [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave"), alongside two other dead bandits in a small alcove.
- At the very bottom of [Fort Sungard Oubliette](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard_Oubliette "Skyrim:Fort Sungard Oubliette"), near the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill book, *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")*.
- Just past the first cages in [Ravenscar Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hollow "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow"), near another dead bandit and a dead [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan").
- In the center of the wolf arena in [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"), alongside two other dead bandits.
- Within the first chamber of [Bonechill Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonechill_Passage "Skyrim:Bonechill Passage"), down near the mammoth skull.
- Two can be found inside of [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast"); one is at the bottom of a pit along with several other dead bandits, while the other can be found locked inside of a cage.
- Near a small alcove slightly southeast of a [Shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrine of Dibella"), with two [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") nearby. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=38537&y=78422)
- Just outside of the entrance leading into [Darkshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkshade "Skyrim:Darkshade"), next to the dead body of a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=81642&y=-1901)
- Washed slightly ashore at the bottom of the waterfall, along with a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=85732&y=-26854)
- On top of a novice-locked chest, slightly southwest of the [Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp"), and near several [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") and a [cave bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear "Skyrim:Cave Bear"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-166352&y=30998)
- Outside the ruins of [Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald"), going past the entrance itself on the left-hand side. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-177619&y=26669)
- Just outside the entrance of [Talking Stone Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Talking_Stone_Camp "Skyrim:Talking Stone Camp"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-69023&y=20345)
- Within a small dead-end passageway overrun with spiderwebs in [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave").
- Within [Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove"), just before the shrine dedicated to [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").[[²]](#intnote_daedric)

[^¹](#note_tg)You can only access this location by initiating the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted").

[^²](#note_daedric)You can only access this location by initiating the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe").

## Redguard Female

| Bandit | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

_11.jpg)

Wolfskull Cave

These **bandits** are all female [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)").

They wear randomly determined [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is a 50% chance it will be [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally,they have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of them carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Their weapon of choice is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). They also carry a bit of random loot, food and drink, with a slim chance of a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- One inside [Fort Snowhawk Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk_Prison "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk Prison"), in a cell.
- In [Sightless Pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Sightless_Pit "Skyrim:Sightless Pit"), at the bottom of the first pit north of the bandit camp.
- In the center of the wolf arena in the [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"), along with two other dead bandits.
- On the eastern side of the waterfall, near the fallen tree acting as a bridge across the river. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=82849&y=-25414)
- Overhead of the entrance leading into [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-95599&y=107395)

_12.jpg)

Lost Knife Hideout

These **bandits** are all male [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)").

They wear randomly determined [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is a 50% chance it will be [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally, they have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of them carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Their weapon of choice is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). They also carry a bit of random loot, food and drink, with a slim chance of a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- In the final chamber of [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame#Haemar.27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame"), near the shrine dedicated to [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile") and with several [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") nearby.
- In the prison corridor of [Fort Greenwall Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall#Fort_Greenwall_Prison "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall"), along with several [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") nearby.[[\*]](#intnote_civilwar)
- In [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair"), in the tunnel east of the first chamber.
- In the main chamber of [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout#Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"), located nearby another dead bandit.
- Near the entrance into [Fort Neugrad Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad#Fort_Neugrad_Prison "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad"), within a cage. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=35187&y=-92353)

[^\*](#note_civilwar)Must not have completed either the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Stormcloaks)") related civil war quests.

## Bosmer Female

| Bandit | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Bandit Archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000328DC |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

_13.jpg)

Silverdrift Lair

These **bandits** are all female [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [bandit archers](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer").

They wear randomly determined [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is a 50% chance it will be [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally,they have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 onward, it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers").

They carry a leveled bow; from level 1-3 it will be either a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") or a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), from level 4, it will be an [Imperial bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow"), from level 10 it will be an [Orcish bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Bow "Skyrim:Orcish Bow"), from level 15 it will be a [Dwarven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bow "Skyrim:Dwarven Bow"), and from level 20 onward, it will be an [elven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Bow "Skyrim:Elven Bow"). The twenty arrows are leveled as well and follow the leveling of the bows. Additionally, they will carry six arrows of the highest possible quality and a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") leveled to elven quality at level 20. They also carry a bit of random loot and some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- In [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt"), inside a locked cell.
- In [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair"), on a bedroll, in the room with the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill book *[Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(book) "Skyrim:Thief (book)")*.
- In [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave"), in the last chamber.

Honeystrand Cave

These **bandits** are all male [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [bandit archers](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer").

They wear randomly determined [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is a 50% chance it will be [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally,they have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 onward, it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers").

They carry a leveled bow; from level 1-3 it will be either a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") or a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), from level 4, it will be an [Imperial bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow"), from level 10 it will be an [Orcish bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Bow "Skyrim:Orcish Bow"), from level 15 it will be a [Dwarven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bow "Skyrim:Dwarven Bow"), and from level 20 onward, it will be an elven bow. The twenty arrows are leveled as well and follow the leveling of the bows. Additionally, they will carry six arrows of the highest possible quality and a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") leveled to elven quality at level 20. They also carry a bit of random loot and some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- One can be found within [Honeystrand Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeystrand_Cave "Skyrim:Honeystrand Cave"), located in the center of the cave itself and with several leveled [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") nearby.
- One can be found within [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat"), located behind a turned over table in the dining area.
- One can be found within [Duskglow Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Duskglow_Crevice "Skyrim:Duskglow Crevice"), located within the third chamber and with a leveled [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") nearby.

_15.jpg)

Shriekwind Bastion

This **bandit** is a female [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who can be found within [Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion") on top of a [ceiling spike trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Ceiling_Spikes "Skyrim:Ceiling Spikes"), which can be activated by pulling a nearby [pull chain](/wiki/Skyrim:Switches "Skyrim:Switches"). This bandit can also be [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie") by a nearby [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire").

She wears a randomly determined set of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is always a 50% chance she will wear [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ for both shoes and armor; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [studded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally, she has a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of her carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Her weapon is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). She always carries some random loot and a bit of gold.

Ilinalta's Deep

This **bandit** is a [bandit archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer") whose race and gender are [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"). She can be found deep within [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep"), usually [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie") by a [master necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Necromancer "Skyrim:Master Necromancer") nearby.

She wears a randomly determined set of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is always a 50% chance she will wear [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ for both shoes and armor; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [studded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally, she has a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of her carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Her weapon is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). She always carries some random loot and a bit of gold.

Additionally, he has a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of him carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Fallowstone Cave

These **bandits** are both male [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"). They have different IDs than their regular Orc [counterparts](#TreasCorpseBanditOrcMale).

They wear randomly determined [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is a 50% chance it will be [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally,they have a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5 there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), and at level 19 it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of them carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

Their weapon of choice is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). He also carries a bit of random loot, food and drink, with a slim chance of a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or some gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

- One can be found within the [bandit sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch_Bandit%27s_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Pinewatch Bandit's Sanctuary") at [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"), located underneath a makeshift bridge overhead in the second chamber.
- One can be found within [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave"), located underneath a small alcove in the second chamber alongside a leveled shield and an enchanted [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe").

He wields a leveled bow; from level 1-3 it will be either a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") or a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), from level 4, it will be an [Imperial bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow"), from level 10 it will be an [Orcish bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Bow "Skyrim:Orcish Bow"), from level 15 it will be a [Dwarven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bow "Skyrim:Dwarven Bow"), and from level 20 onward, it will be an [elven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Bow "Skyrim:Elven Bow"). The twenty arrows are leveled as well and follow the leveling of the bows. Additionally, he will carry six arrows of the highest possible quality and a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") leveled to elven quality at level 20. He also carries a bit of random loot and some gold.

Liar's Retreat

This **bandit** is a female [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [bandit wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") who can be found dead behind the counter in the dining area of [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat").

She wears a set of [tavern clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tavern_Clothes "Skyrim:Tavern Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000d1921 "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and has a slim chance of carrying a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or some gold. Despite her condition, she also knows a few spells, specifically [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward"), [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), and the three standard [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells, [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"), [Frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite "Skyrim:Frostbite"), and [Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks").

# Skyrim:Bandit Attack

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

The ransom note

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Kill the bandits attacking your home.
2. Read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ransom_Note "Skyrim:Ransom Note") to discover where your spouse is.
3. Rescue your spouse through violence, or pay the ransom.

## Detailed Walkthrough

At some point you may arrive at your newly constructed house to find a group of bandits attacking it. Kill the bandits and then loot them to discover a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ransom_Note "Skyrim:Ransom Note") that explains why they were attacking. You will discover that your spouse has been kidnapped by [Rochelle the Red](/wiki/Skyrim:Rochelle_the_Red "Skyrim:Rochelle the Red"), and she is demanding 5,000 gold for your spouse's safe release.

Travel to Rochelle's hideout, as indicated by the note, and make your choice to deal with the situation through violence or by paying the ransom. If you pay the ransom, your spouse will be safely returned to you. If you choose violence, you will need to kill all the bandits in the dungeon to safely rescue your loved one.

### Radiant Options

The bandit camp will be in the same [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") as the house from which your spouse was taken.

| [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall") | [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor") | [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor") |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt") | [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine") [Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep") [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine") [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge") | [Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim") [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") |

## Notes

- This quest will not occur unless your spouse is living in one of the three constructable homes added by Hearthfire, nor (obviously) will it occur if your spouse is currently following you.
- This quest will also not occur if your spouse is any of the following people:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Argis the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:Argis_the_Bulwark "Skyrim:Argis the Bulwark") [Athis](/wiki/Skyrim:Athis "Skyrim:Athis") [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor") [Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart") [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach") [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") | [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") [Jenassa](/wiki/Skyrim:Jenassa "Skyrim:Jenassa") [Octieve San](/wiki/Skyrim:Octieve_San "Skyrim:Octieve San") [Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag") [Perth](/wiki/Skyrim:Perth "Skyrim:Perth") [Romlyn Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth") [Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") | [Shahvee](/wiki/Skyrim:Shahvee "Skyrim:Shahvee") [Sondas Drenim](/wiki/Skyrim:Sondas_Drenim "Skyrim:Sondas Drenim") [Stenvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Stenvar "Skyrim:Stenvar") [Torvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Torvar "Skyrim:Torvar") [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano") [Vorstag](/wiki/Skyrim:Vorstag "Skyrim:Vorstag") |

- If you have a [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") ([Gregor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gregor "Skyrim:Gregor"), [Rayya](/wiki/Skyrim:Rayya "Skyrim:Rayya"), or [Valdimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdimar "Skyrim:Valdimar")) staying in the house where your spouse is, or if any of these are your spouse[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Bandit_Attack)*], Rochelle the Red will attack you outside your home rather than kidnapping your spouse.

## Bugs

- The quest may automatically complete itself. If this happens your spouse should be at your home.
  - The best solution is to load an earlier save after reading the location of the bandits and go directly there instead of going to your home.
- Whether the quest has been completed or not, your spouse may become badly bugged and walk backwards.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Return to a save that is far back enough that the quest has not been triggered, and move your spouse to a city.
  -  You can solve this bug by opening the console, clicking on your spouse, and using the `resurrect` command.
  -  If your spouse becomes bugged somewhere other than home, you can find them by using `player.moveto <RefID#>`. Nudging the spouse might set them back on the path, but they will still be bugged when arriving home.
- For Console Players: Revert to save before Bandit Ransom quest. Do the quest "Rescue" given by Florentius in Fort Dawnguard. Initiate the quest and your spouse should move to the Vampire's lair. Save your spouse from Vampires and follow them out of trapped location. Eventually your spouse's dialogue tree resets and you can ask your spouse to move to one of the city homes. This should avoid the backwards walking glitch entirely.
- Some bandits may be hostile, either causing Rochelle to turn hostile as well, or attacking you while you're talking with her.
- Rochelle's Intimidate options are not marked as such.
- Although technically a repeatable quest, it will only repeat once every 50,000 hours or a bit less than six in-game years.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The spouse may be "rescued" before the quest ever begins if you adopt a child. If you choose for your new child to reside in a different house than your spouse, the spouse will be sent to the new house. There, your spouse will speak as if you're just then rescuing them, before resuming normal dialogue. Bandits are found attacking your spouse's original home, where you can get the quest in your journal. The quest auto-completes before too long. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Bandit Attack (BYOHHouseBanditAttack2) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 40 |  | *Objective 5:* Read the bandit's ransom note for <Alias=Spouse> |
| 50 |  | *Objective 10:* Rescue <Alias=Spouse> from <Alias=BanditDungeon> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5, 10, 20, 30, 60, 70, 80, 100, 120, 150, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BYOHHouseBanditAttack2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BYOHHouseBanditAttack2`.

# Skyrim:Bandit Leader

## Overview

| Bandit Leader (RefID: 000430B5) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Mistwatch East Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_East_Tower "Skyrim:Mistwatch East Tower") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | PC×1.1 (min=5) | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000430B5 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00090739 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 38⅓+level×11⅔ | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 46⅔+level×3⅓ | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [dunMistwatchFjolaFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DunMistwatchFjolaFaction "Skyrim:DunMistwatchFjolaFaction") | | |

Fjola as the bandit leader in Mistwatch

**Fjola**, the secret name of the **Bandit Leader** of [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch"), is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), whose aging husband [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") will ask you to find her during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)"). However, Fjola has made a drastic career change and it is up to you to figure out how to solve it peacefully.

She wears a leveled set of [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), which can be up to [steel plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor") (or [Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Armor "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Armor") with Dragonborn add-on installed) in quality. She wields a leveled [one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") weapon with a chance of a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), both of which may be up to [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") in quality. She also carries a spare leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") that may be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality, and a leveled amount of gold.

She can be found in [Mistwatch East Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_East_Tower "Skyrim:Mistwatch East Tower"), from where she commands the [Mistwatch bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit") that protect the ruin. She just wanders around, without ever sleeping or eating, and will actively seek you out the moment you enter her premises.

## Related Quests

- **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)")**: Help [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") locate his kidnapped wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola").

## Quest-Related Events

When she approaches you she will ask:

:   *"All right, snowback. Who are you, and what are you doing in my tower?"*
:   **Stand aside, woman. I'm here for Fjola!**
:   *"Fjola? How do you know that name?"*
:   **Her husband sent me. Where is she?**
:   *"Christer? He's here?"*
:   **Wait. You know him?**
:   *"The fool's my husband. I'm Fjola - or I was, once. Don't you see? I left that old scab. Came home to Skyrim, and found this rabble of bandits. Didn't take much to prove myself and knock them into shape. Now every free blade from here to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") wants to sign on for a piece."*
:   **That's quite a story.**
:   *"And it won't end here. I'd die before I went back."*

At this point, three options are available to you, with different outcomes:

| Topic | Dialogue | Outcome |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **There's no way you'll come peacefully?** | *"None. Not back to him."* | Dialogue option disappears. |
| **This is pointless. I should just kill you and be done with it.** | *"Better men have tried. Let's finish this."* **or**  *"You think so? Let's see who the real woman is here."* | Draws weapon and attacks. |
| **What am I supposed to tell Christer?** | *"I don't know. I never expected the old bag to follow me so far. Just get rid of him. But don't kill him. I don't hate the man. I just want him to go back to his farm and forget about me."* | A new topic appears. |

If you choose not to fight her, a new topic will appear. If you assure her you will get him to leave Mistwatch she will hand you her [wedding band](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola%27s_Wedding_Band "Skyrim:Fjola's Wedding Band"):

:   '**ll try getting him to leave.**
:   *"Take my wedding band. [Stuhn](/wiki/Lore:Stuhn "Lore:Stuhn") only knows why I've kept it this long. He'll recognize it. Tell him whatever you think will convince him to leave. The ring itself is worth a few bits. Keep it as thanks for cutting off the last vestige of an unwanted fate."*

If you speak with her before confronting Christer, she will ask:

:   *"I didn't expect to see you again. What became of my doting husband?"*
:   **I haven't dealt with him yet.**
:   *"Then stop wasting my time."*

After dealing with Christer, you must return to Fjola to finish the quest. Regardless of how you dealt with her husband, she will be grateful:

:   **He won't bother you again.**
:   *"How did... no, forget it. I don't care to know. I'm free of the little man, and that's what matters. I owe you a debt, and I aim to repay it. We'll see each other again someday. For now, goodbye, and thanks."*

## Notes

- The game actually presents her as "Bandit Leader", so you might accidentally kill her.
- Fjola will engage you in conversation even if you just killed all of her crew.
- You won't actually see her again unless you come back to Mistwatch. Nor will she ever actually repay any favors that she says she owes you.
- If you help Fjola, the bandits at Mistwatch will no longer become hostile towards you.
- If you kill Fjola, Christer will call you a "monster" for doing so, and immediately become hostile.
- If you cast a calm spell on Christer once he attacks you and leave the building then you will get the other two options when speaking to him next time you meet.

## Bugs

See [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest)#Bugs "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)").

# Skyrim:Bandit Thief

## Overview

In the original version of the [Divine Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), two **Bandit Thieves** could be found at [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout"). They had stolen the Crusader's Relics and were killed during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Relics_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Relics of the Crusader"). However with the release of [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), the creation was reworked so that the relics are found on two dead NPCs, [Eigorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Eigorn "Skyrim:Eigorn") and [Oren](/wiki/Skyrim:Oren "Skyrim:Oren"), as it did not fit the lore of the Crusader's Relics for bandits to be able to wear them.

## Related Quests

- **[Relics of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Relics_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Relics of the Crusader")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader"): Reclaim the holy relics of Pelinal Whitestrake.

# Skyrim:Bandit

## Overview

For dead NPCs named "Bandit", see [Bandit (dead)](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead) "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)"). For other uses, see [Bandit (disambiguation)](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(disambiguation) "Skyrim:Bandit (disambiguation)").

Bandits

**Bandits** are rogue lawbreakers living a life of plunder and are one of the most common enemy types in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). You will typically find them in camps, some of which are [marked](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") on your map, and some of which are [unmarked](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Unmarked_Bandit_and_Forsworn_Camps "Skyrim:Unmarked Places"). Of the marked locations, bandits often inhabit both the interiors and exteriors of fort-type and other structures.

Although most bandits will attack you on sight, some may attack only when you get too close. Still others will demand that you pay them and attack if you refuse. Bandits can be members of any race (except [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf")), and may be spellcasters, archers, one-handed melee fighters, or two-handed melee fighters.

## Bandit Types

While the stronger bandit types will not appear until after you've reached the levels shown, you will continue to meet low-level versions even at high levels. Boss-level bandits will always be at the highest possible level, and will normally be identified as "Bandit Chief". Bandits of each type may vary in the combat equipment and style they use.

Normal Bandits are generally fairly easy to kill, while Bandit Chiefs and Marauders are tougher. Unlike other Bandit Marauders, Bandit Marauder mages (bandits with the [Bandit Wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") class) begin appearing at level 24.

### One-Handed Melee

These bandits wield one-handed melee weapons and shields in battle. They carry one of the following weapons, depending on your level:

- **Mace:** [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), [Orcish mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Mace "Skyrim:Orcish Mace"), [Dwarven mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Mace "Skyrim:Dwarven Mace"), [Elven mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Mace "Skyrim:Elven Mace") or [Nordic mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Mace "Skyrim:Nordic Mace")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Sword:** [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), [orcish sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Sword "Skyrim:Orcish Sword"), [Dwarven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sword "Skyrim:Dwarven Sword"), [Elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword") or [Nordic sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Sword "Skyrim:Nordic Sword")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **War Axe:** [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"), [Orcish war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_War_Axe "Skyrim:Orcish War Axe"), [Dwarven war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dwarven War Axe"), [Elven war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Elven War Axe") or [Nordic war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_War_Axe "Skyrim:Nordic War Axe")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

All bandits also carry a random assortment of items, which include [beverages](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food"), [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), tools, [ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots"), and a small amount of gold. Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry more gold and may carry additional lockpicks.

#### Light Armor

A Bandit Marauder looking for trouble

In addition to the weapons listed above, these bandits wear a set of leveled light armor:

- **Cuirass:** [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), [studded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor"), [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor"), or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor")
- **Boots:** [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes"), [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), or [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots")
- **Gauntlets:** 50% chance of [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers"), [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), or [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers")
- **Shield:** 20% chance of a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"), [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), or [elven shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Shield "Skyrim:Elven Shield")

[^1](#note_NotArcher)This male Redguard bandit (`EncBandit01Melee1HRedguardM`) also appears in the list of level 1 archers (`SubCharBandit01Missile`), but has all the stats and inventory appropriate for a one-handed weapon fighter.

[^2](#note_Level0)These Bandit Highwaymen are actually set as level 0; they have lower health and stamina than other bandits that appear when you are the appropriate level. If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, their level and stats will be corrected (hover to see values).

#### Heavy Armor

A Bandit Thug in full steel armor

These bandits wield one-handed melee weapons and shields in battle. They carry the same weapons and miscellaneous items as their light armor counterparts, and wear a set of leveled heavy armor:

- **Cuirass:** [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), [steel plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor"), or [Nordic carved armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Armor "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Armor")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Boots:** [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots"), [steel plate boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Plate Boots"), or [Nordic carved boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Boots "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Boots")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Gauntlets:** 50% chance of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets"), [steel Imperial gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Imperial_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Imperial Gauntlets"), [steel plate gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Plate Gauntlets"), or [Nordic carved gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Gauntlets")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Helmet:** [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet"), [steel horned helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Horned_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Horned Helmet"), [steel plate helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Plate Helmet"), or [Nordic carved helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Helmet "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Helmet")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Shield:** [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"), [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), or [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield")

### Two-Handed Melee

A Bandit fighter wielding his fearsome greatsword

These bandits carry large, two-handed melee weapons into the fray. They wear the same leveled armor as their one-handed light armored counterparts (without the shield), and also carry one of the following weapons, depending on your level:

- **Battleaxe:** [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe"), [Orcish battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Orcish Battleaxe"), [Dwarven battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Dwarven Battleaxe"), [Elven battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Elven Battleaxe") or [Nordic battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Nordic Battleaxe")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Greatsword:** [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword"), [Orcish greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Greatsword "Skyrim:Orcish Greatsword"), [Dwarven greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Greatsword "Skyrim:Dwarven Greatsword"), [Elven greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Greatsword "Skyrim:Elven Greatsword") or [Nordic greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Greatsword "Skyrim:Nordic Greatsword")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Warhammer:** [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer"), [Orcish warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Warhammer "Skyrim:Orcish Warhammer"), [Dwarven warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Warhammer "Skyrim:Dwarven Warhammer"), [Elven warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Warhammer "Skyrim:Elven Warhammer") or [Nordic warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Warhammer "Skyrim:Nordic Warhammer")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

Two-handed melee bandits also carry a small amount of gold and have a chance to carry a few lockpicks. Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry an [orcish dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger") and have no lockpicks.

[^1](#note_Berserker)These two-handed melee bandits appear in "berserker" leveled lists; they are identical to other two-handed fighters, except that they have a morality of `No Crime` instead of `Any Crime` and have the `csHumanBerserkerLvl1` fighting style instead of `csHumanMeleeLvl1`.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") fixes this bug.

[^2](#note_AlsoLevel5)`SubCharBandit01Melee2HBerserk` and `SubCharBandit02Melee2HBerserk` contain the same list of bandits, which means the berserkers that appear in the level 1 list also appear in the level 5 list (with stats and perks appropriate for level 1 bandits).

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.

### Archers

A Bandit Marauder drawing a deadly arrow

Archer bandits prefer to keep their distance, using a bow and arrows to attack. These bandits have the [Bandit Archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer") class. They wear the same leveled armor as [melee bandits](#One-Handed_Melee), and also one of each of the following weapon types, depending on your level:

- **Bow:** [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), [Imperial bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow"), [Orcish bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Bow "Skyrim:Orcish Bow"), [Dwarven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bow "Skyrim:Dwarven Bow"), [Elven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Bow "Skyrim:Elven Bow") or [Nordic bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Bow "Skyrim:Nordic Bow")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Arrows (20):** [iron arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [Orcish arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [Dwarven arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), [Elven arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow") or [Nordic arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Arrow "Skyrim:Nordic Arrow")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Dagger:** [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [Orcish dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [Dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [Elven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger") or [Nordic dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dagger "Skyrim:Nordic Dagger")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

Archers carry the same miscellaneous loot as their one-handed counterparts, and also have a small chance of carrying additional arrows of any type (including [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Arrow "Skyrim:Glass Arrow"), [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Arrow "Skyrim:Ebony Arrow"), and [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Arrow "Skyrim:Daedric Arrow")). Archer Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry more gold than those at lower levels.

[^2](#note_Cat)None of the Khajiit archers can actually appear in-game as they never got added to the respective leveled list.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

### Mages

A bandit mage dual-wielding shock spells

Bandit mages rely primarily on spellcasting in battle. They wear the following leveled armor:

- **Cuirass:** [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor")
- **Boots:** [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes"), [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), or [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots")

Bandit and Bandit Outlaw mages carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), while Bandit Thug mages carry a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). Bandit Highwayman, Bandit Plunderer, and Bandit Marauder mages carry a leveled dagger ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), or [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger")).

In addition to their gear, bandit mages carry a random assortment of items, including [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves"), and a small amount of gold. Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry more gold and have a chance to carry additional lockpicks than lower-level mages.
