[^1](#note_MagickaRecovery2)"Magicka Recovery 2" is an ability that increases magicka regeneration by 2%. This perk is available to NPCs only.

[^2](#note_Level24)Bandit Marauder mages begin appearing when the player is level 24, rather than level 25 like the other bandit types.

### One-Handed Melee Bandit Chiefs

A Redguard Bandit Chief ready for battle

Bandit Chiefs use the same fighting style as other melee bandits, but are a higher level, which means they have more health, more stamina, and more perks. All Bandit Chiefs carry a leveled dagger ([steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), or [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger")) in addition to one of the following weapons:

- **Mace:** [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), enchanted [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), [Orcish mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Mace "Skyrim:Orcish Mace"), enchanted steel mace, enchanted Orcish mace, [Dwarven mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Mace "Skyrim:Dwarven Mace"), enchanted Dwarven mace, [Elven mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Mace "Skyrim:Elven Mace"), enchanted Elven mace, [Nordic mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Mace "Skyrim:Nordic Mace")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), enchanted Nordic mace [glass mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Mace "Skyrim:Glass Mace"), enchanted glass mace, or [ebony mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Mace "Skyrim:Ebony Mace")
- **Sword:** [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), enchanted [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), [Orcish sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Sword "Skyrim:Orcish Sword"), enchanted steel sword, enchanted Orcish sword, [Dwarven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sword "Skyrim:Dwarven Sword"), enchanted Dwarven sword, [Elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword"), enchanted Elven sword, [Nordic sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Sword "Skyrim:Nordic Sword")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), enchanted Nordic sword, [glass sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Sword "Skyrim:Glass Sword"), enchanted glass sword, or [ebony sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Sword "Skyrim:Ebony Sword")
- **War Axe:** [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"), enchanted [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), [Orcish war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_War_Axe "Skyrim:Orcish War Axe"), enchanted steel war axe, enchanted Orcish war axe, [Dwarven war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dwarven War Axe"), enchanted Dwarven war axe, [Elven war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Elven War Axe"), enchanted Elven war axe, [Nordic war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_War_Axe "Skyrim:Nordic War Axe")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), enchanted Nordic war axe, [glass war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_War_Axe "Skyrim:Glass War Axe"), enchanted glass war axe, or [ebony war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_War_Axe "Skyrim:Ebony War Axe")

The enchanted weapons listed above will have either [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"), [frost damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage"), [shock damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage"), [magicka damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka_Damage "Skyrim:Magicka Damage"), or [stamina damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina_Damage "Skyrim:Stamina Damage") enchantments. The strength of the enchantment will vary depending on the level of the item.

Bandit Chiefs wear the following leveled heavy armor:

- **Cuirass:** [banded iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor"), [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), [steel plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor"), or [Nordic carved armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Armor "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Armor")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Boots:** [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots"), [steel shin boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shin_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Shin Boots"), [steel plate boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Plate Boots"), or [Nordic carved boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Boots "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Boots")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Gauntlets:** 50% chance of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets"), [steel Imperial gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Imperial_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Imperial Gauntlets"), [steel plate gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Plate Gauntlets"), or [Nordic carved gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Gauntlets")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Helmet:** 50% chance of [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet"), [steel horned helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Horned_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Horned Helmet"), [steel plate helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Plate Helmet"), or [Nordic carved helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Helmet "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Helmet")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **Shield:** [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield"), [dwarven shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Shield "Skyrim:Dwarven Shield"), [orcish shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Shield "Skyrim:Orcish Shield"), [ebony shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Shield "Skyrim:Ebony Shield"), or [Nordic shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Shield "Skyrim:Nordic Shield")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

In addition to the equipment listed above, all Bandit Chiefs carry a leveled amount of gold.

[^2](#note_TwoHanded)These Bandit Chiefs have `LItemBanditWeapon2HBoss` instead of `LItemBanditBossWeapon1H`, so they actually carry two-handed weapons.

[^3](#note_LessHealth)This Bandit Chief has only 282 health instead of 395.

[^4](#note_OrcishDagger)Bandit Chiefs at this level should have an elven dagger, but this one has an orcish dagger.

### Two-Handed Melee Bandit Chiefs

A Bandit Chief in steel plate armor, wielding his glass greatsword

These Bandit Chiefs wear the same heavy armor as their one-handed allies (without the shield). They carry a leveled dagger ([steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), or [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger")) in addition to one of the following weapons:

- **Battleaxe:** [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe"), enchanted [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), [Orcish battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Orcish Battleaxe"), enchanted steel battleaxe, enchanted Orcish battleaxe, [Dwarven battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Dwarven Battleaxe"), enchanted Dwarven battleaxe, [Elven battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Elven Battleaxe"), enchanted Elven battleaxe, [Nordic battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Nordic Battleaxe")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), enchanted Nordic battleaxe, [glass battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Glass Battleaxe"), enchanted glass battleaxe, or [ebony battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Ebony Battleaxe")
- **Greatsword:** [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword"), enchanted [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), [Orcish greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Greatsword "Skyrim:Orcish Greatsword"), enchanted steel greatsword, enchanted Orcish greatsword, [Dwarven greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Greatsword "Skyrim:Dwarven Greatsword"), enchanted Dwarven greatsword, [Elven greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Greatsword "Skyrim:Elven Greatsword"), enchanted Elven greatsword, [Nordic greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Greatsword "Skyrim:Nordic Greatsword")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), enchanted Nordic greatsword, [glass greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Greatsword "Skyrim:Glass Greatsword"), enchanted glass greatsword, or [ebony greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Greatsword "Skyrim:Ebony Greatsword")
- **Warhammer:** [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer"), enchanted [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), [Orcish warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Warhammer "Skyrim:Orcish Warhammer"), enchanted steel warhammer, enchanted Orcish warhammer, [Dwarven warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Warhammer "Skyrim:Dwarven Warhammer"), enchanted Dwarven warhammer, [Elven warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Warhammer "Skyrim:Elven Warhammer"), enchanted Elven warhammer, [Nordic warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Warhammer "Skyrim:Nordic Warhammer")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), enchanted Nordic warhammer, [glass warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Warhammer "Skyrim:Glass Warhammer"), enchanted glass warhammer, or [ebony warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warhammer "Skyrim:Ebony Warhammer")

The enchanted weapons listed above will have either [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"), [frost damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage"), [shock damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage"), [magicka damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka_Damage "Skyrim:Magicka Damage"), or [stamina damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina_Damage "Skyrim:Stamina Damage") enchantments. The strength of the enchantment will vary depending on the level of the item.

### Mistwatch Bandits

[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch") contains a group of bandits called Mistwatch Bandits; these location-specific bandits can be either [one-handed melee fighters](#One-Handed_Melee), [two-handed melee fighters](#Two-Handed_Melee), [archers](#Archers), or [mages](#Mages), and have the same stats and perks as their ordinary bandit counterparts. They are all members of the [Mistwatch faction](/wiki/Skyrim:DunMistwatchFaction "Skyrim:DunMistwatchFaction"), and will no longer be hostile towards the player should the [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)") quest be completed in [Fjola's](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola") favor.

## Related Quests

Some quests that require going into a bandit hideout or dungeon include:

- **[Infiltration](/wiki/Skyrim:Infiltration "Skyrim:Infiltration")**: Help [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") take back [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch").
- **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)")**: Help [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") locate his kidnapped wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola").
- **[Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining")**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") for a [silversmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon").
- **[Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand")**: Clear [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
- **[The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")**: Find out what happened in [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt").

### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Bandit Boss](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Bandit_Boss "Skyrim:Bounty: Bandit Boss")**: Eliminate a bandit leader for a bounty reward.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout.
- **[Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master")**: Take care of a runaway crew member.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader.
- **[Rescue Mission](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to rescue a kidnapped citizen.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

Bandits gathered around a table

If you speak to a bandit who is leaning against a wall, typically guarding the outside of a hideout, they may give a generic, non-hostile response (such as *"You need something?"*), although after a few seconds they will draw their weapon and attack. Male bandits will talk to themselves while idle, but they do not talk to each other unless scripted by a certain location [*verification needed — verify males only*].

### Idling

- *"...retire some day... get myself an island..."*
- *"...never enough gold... just need one good haul..."*
- *"...might pay off my bounty this time... walk into the city a free man..."*
- *"...told him to just hand over the gold, but did he listen? Oh, no... they always have to fight back..."*
- *"...I'll never do another span in that stinking jail... rather die than give myself up..."*
- *"...he he he... two threes? What was he thinking? Fool never saw me pull that ace out of my boot..."*
- *"[Sighing] ...need me some Skooma... the imported stuff... just one last time..."*
- *"...gonna start keepin' a knife in my boot... tired of gettin' disarmed..."*
- *"...should have known she was lying... said she'd wait for me... but they never wait..."*
- *"...lyin' little harlot... that brat ain't mine... could be anyone's... won't get one rusty septim from me..."*
- *"..."go to the college" da said... "use your smarts" he said... like I'm supposed to figure out which college he meant..."*
- *"...hmph, wizards... Now that's power... Bet they got that "secret" magic... can turn wood to gold... yeah... Wish I could turn wood to gold..."*
- *"...mead, mead, mead... kill him to get some beer every now and then? Stupid bees and their stupid honey..."*
- *"...picking pockets, now that's the real art... ...no rough stuff, just take it and go... ...hmph, don't sound like much fun, though..."*
- *"[Singing] ...once was a woman, as fair as an evenin', of springtime in old Stros M'Kai..."*
- *"[Singing] ...with three beers down, the Orc did frown, and bid the Elf goodbye... ...for none could know, 'twas not for show, and someone had to die..."*
- *"...kill 'em, he talks to me again like that... get him when he's sleeping... or poison his meat... see how he likes that."*

### Combat

- *"Never should have come here!"*
- *"Lookee here. Looks like we got ourselves a hero."*
- *"You picked a bad time to get lost, friend."*
- *"Now ain't this a surprise."*
- *"Time to die, hero!"*
- *"Go ahead, try and fight back!"*
- *"Die already so I can take your stuff!"*
- *"Whatcha gonna do? Huh? Whatcha gonna do?"*
- *"Gonna split your belly like an old woman's purse!"*
- *"Gonna rip you... open!"*
- *"You'll be so much easier to rob when you're dead..."*
- *"Tell you what. You start running so I can stab you in the back."*
- *"Can't wait to count out your coin..."*

### Miscellaneous

A male bandit who has just discovered a corpse may say:

- *"What...? Whoever did this, you're dead. You hear me? Dead!"*

When playing as a Khajiit, a bandit may say:

- *"You'll make a fine rug, cat!"*

### Location Specific Dialogue

In Lost Knife Cave, you can hear two bandits having a conversation:

**Bandit #1:** *"So, you're saying you brought that cat down alone?"*

**Bandit #2:** *"Why, you don't think I could do it?"*

**Bandit #1:** *"Wasn't our last catch a cave bear?"*

**Bandit #2:** *"Yeah, why?"*

**Bandit #1:** *"Take down that one with your bare hands too?"*

**Bandit #2:** *"Troll's blood was he a tough one!"*

**Bandit #1:** *"pfft"*

**Bandit #2:** *"But, I've got the key to the Sabre cage. Look!"*

**Bandit #1:** *"What's that supposed to prove? Get back on patrol!"*

## Notes

- Bandits encountered in Skyrim are generally twice as likely to be male than female. In most cases, the leveled lists that spawn bandits list each male bandit twice (except Khajiits) and each female bandit once.
- Most bandits have a [morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") of "Any Crime", which means they're willing to commit any crime. Bandit Chiefs and the "berserker" variety of two-handed fighters, however, have a morality of "No Crime", which means they are unwilling to commit crimes of any sort. Their aggression is the same as any other bandit, though, so they will still attack you on sight.
- Bandits that spawn within the exterior zone of [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") are set to spawn at a normal leveled list corresponding to your game level. However, bandits which spawn within the interior zone are set to appear 5 levels earlier, which means that at lower levels you will more likely encounter Bandit Marauders, etc.
- There is a bandit imprisoned in [Ravenscar Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hollow "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow") who has been locked up by [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") and will ask you to free him. If he survives the fight with the hagravens, he will demand all of your belongings and you will be forced to kill him. This bandit is one of the few with whom you can exchange more than a couple of lines of conversation.
- [Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") adds entries for level 48 characters in Bandit Bosses' leveled list, these characters wear [Daedric Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Daedric Mail") armor.
- The *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* add-on makes it possible for high level bandits to appear with [Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic "Skyrim:Nordic") weapons and/or Nordic Carved Armor.
- Version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") members at [Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge") with regular bandits once the dungeon resets after [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge") is finished.
- Bandit Chiefs that spawn with a shield will bash you far more often than those who spawn with just a one-handed weapon, or two-handed versions of chiefs. Standard one-handed weapon and shield bandits also do not bash as much as their counterpart bandit chiefs do. It is quite possible to be stun-locked by a bandit chief with a shield, as they bash quickly and very often in quick succession.

## Bugs

- Once the bandits in [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") arrive, they respawn despite the area being a "no-reset zone".
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Bannermist Tower

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Tower.png) | Nordic Tower: Bannermist Tower ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bannermist+Tower)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |

| Special Features | |
| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |

Bannermist Tower

**Bannermist Tower** is a small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)")**: Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

One bandit patrols outside the tower. Off the path leading up to the tower, to the south, is a birds' nest containing a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), with a second nest with another egg at the western base of the tower. A vacant [beehive](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive_Husk "Skyrim:Beehive Husk") hangs underneath the entrance ramp, while a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") are by the foot of the tower to the south. The entrance ramp is at the rear of the tower, lodged between the tower and the hill.

Bannermist Tower

Just before the entrance ramp, at the base of the tower, is an apprentice-locked gate to the storage area. Inside are an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a table beside it holding a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two [garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), and four loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). The stairs down end in a cave-in where there are two patches of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus.

The first level at the top of the entrance ramp holds only sacks and barrels of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and two bedrolls, one of which is often occupied by a sleeping bandit. On the second level of the tower, across a plank walkway, are a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), various crates, sacks, and barrels, and a small wooden table holding a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Advances in Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Advances_in_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Advances in Lockpicking")* (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Also, there is a weapon rack holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") (which may have fallen to the floor). An unlocked chest is tucked away beneath the stairs behind more barrels and sacks leading up to the top level. The top level is simply a lookout station, and usually contains a bandit, with a small table where a copy of a random [common book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") has been left for some light reading while enjoying the scenery, and three loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on the floor.

## Bugs

- The skill book may have fallen through the table and floor and be found near the entrance by the top of the ramp. **?**
  - If you look at the floor directly under where the book appear to be on the table, the "read" prompt should appear.
- The chests here tend to respawn every 5 hours, instead of every 10 or 30 days. For example, if you loot the chests, fast travel to the [city of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), and then fast travel back to Bannermist Tower, only 5 or 6 in-game hours will have passed, but you will find that the chests will have already refilled themselves by then.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=22914)) Their encounter zone setting was incorrectly set to BannermistZone, which caused them to reset so quickly. Their encounter zone has been corrected, and they now properly reset with the rest of the dungeon.

# Skyrim:Banning

## Overview

| Banning (RefID: 0009A7A9) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0009A7A9 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0009A7A8 |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionReach](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach "Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach"); [Favor001QuestGiverFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:Favor001QuestGiverFaction "Skyrim:Favor001QuestGiverFaction"); [JobAnimalTrainerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:JobAnimalTrainerFaction "Skyrim:JobAnimalTrainerFaction"); [JobMerchantFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:JobMerchantFaction "Skyrim:JobMerchantFaction"); [MarkarthStablesFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthStablesFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthStablesFaction"); [TownMarkarthFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction "Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction") | | |

Banning

**Banning** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") who lives with [Cedran](/wiki/Skyrim:Cedran "Skyrim:Cedran") at the [Markarth Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Markarth Stables") selling war dogs. A [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") named [Vigilance](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilance "Skyrim:Vigilance") can be bought from him for 500 gold. You can make a [delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery") to [Voada](/wiki/Skyrim:Voada "Skyrim:Voada") on his behalf. He is also one of the guests of [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death").

He wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") with [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and matching [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"). He carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), some [small change](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor_Pocket_Contents "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and the [key to the Markarth Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Key to Markarth Stables"). He wakes up at 6am to have breakfast. At 8am, he heads outside to tend to his dogs for a long twelve hours, skipping dinner due to an oversight (see [bugs](#Bugs)). He can be found inside the stables at any other time, and he goes to bed at midnight. Banning also knows the spell  [Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar").

## Related Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

## Dialogue

He'll greet you by advertising his dogs:

:   *"Need a trained war dog? Fiercest companion money can buy."*
:   *"A war dog is good company and good protection."*
:   *"I like the loyalty of a dog. Not as fickle as a wolf."*
:   *"You have to train a good war dog from a pup. Bite your arm clean off otherwise."*

If you have completed The Taste of Death he will greet you with:

:   *"I can smell the blood. Good and sour."*

You can then ask him about the feast:

:   **You were at Namira's feast, weren't you?**
:   *"Better if we don't talk about that. As far as anyone's concerned, we all had dinner at a nice inn along the road, and nothing strange happened."*

If Cedran has passed away, Banning will take over the stables and gain the ability to sell you a horse:

:   *"I'll be handling the horses with Cedran gone. Miss that old man."*

When spoken to directly he can be asked about the city:

:   **What can you tell me about Markarth?**
:   *"Don't fall."*

You can purchase one of his dogs:

:   **I'll take that dog off your hands.**
:   *"Good. Here you are. He'll follow you to [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion") and back, if it comes to that."*

If you try to buy one when you already have a pet follower, he'll refuse your purchase:

:   *"Sorry. You already have an animal with you."*

Similarly, if you don't have enough gold:

:   *"War dogs cost gold, friend. Come back when you have some."*

## Conversations

*"How are the new breeds getting along with my dogs?"*

He can occasionally be found talking with Cedran concerning their business:

**Cedran**: *"Think we should buy more horses next season?"*
**Banning**: *"I'd rather spend the gold on a new litter of pups, but the horses bring in more gold."*

**Banning**: *"How are the new breeds getting along with my dogs?"*
**Cedran**: *"Haven't attacked each other yet. Good a sign as any."*

### Delivery

If you aren't on another [delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery"):

:   **How long have you been training dogs?**
:   *"My family has been doing it for years. You need one out in the [Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). Don't want to be alone when some [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") comes swinging. I personally trained a whole litter for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"). That reminds me, I was going to deliver some dog food to the [Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"). [Spiced beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Beef "Skyrim:Spiced Beef"). Their favorite."*

You can then accept or decline to help:

:   **I could deliver that for you.**

    :   *"Well, look at you, thanks. Take it to Voada, she handles all the dogs for the Jarl."*

:   **That's a shame.**

    :   *"Yeah, yeah."*

### The Taste of Death

*"When was your first meal, Banning?"*

Banning is found sitting at the dinner table. If you talk to him, he'll greet you with:

:   *"I remember my first feast. I envy you."*
:   **Wait, I know you.**
:   *"You buy a war dog from me? There's a reason why my hounds are so eager to bite into people."*

If you've delivered his spiced beef before, he'll recognize you as well:

:   *"Ah, yes. The courier. I guess you know my secret ingredient for that spiced beef, now."*

If you've completed the feast successfully, he may subsequently greet you with:

:   *"You were given [Namira's ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Namira "Skyrim:Ring of Namira")? A great honor."*

He will also randomly engage in conversation with hostess [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola") and fellow Markarth citizens [Hogni Red-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hogni_Red-Arm "Skyrim:Hogni Red-Arm") and [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet"):

**Eola**: *"Not too full on bread and wine, I hope?"*
**Banning**: *"I always leave room for the main course, Eola."*

**Hogni**: *"When was your first meal, Banning?"*
**Banning**: *"Do dogs count?"*
**Hogni**: *"Of course they don't count!"*
**Banning**: *"My friend Marex. We were hunting, and I thought he was an elk."*
**Hogni**: *"That must have been quite a surprise."*
**Banning**: *"Either way, I came back with meat for the table."*

**Lisbet**: *"It's so good to have everyone around the table again."*
**Banning**: *"Eola is a fine host. She really keeps the faithful together."*
**Lisbet**: *"I'm just glad we had this, now. I was almost getting ready to eat my servant and blame it on the Forsworn."*

## Unused Dialogue

According to dialogue found in the game's DialogueViews files, Banning was at one point meant to have a minor role in [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy"), but only if Cedran had passed away. Although the point at which the dialogue would be available is unknown, you would have been able to ask him about a possible Forsworn escape plan.

:   **I need to know if [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach") ever came to you about getting horses.**
:   *"Hmmm... I remember Cedran was talking about a man named Madanach once. I was supposed to be scrubbing the horses, but I heard Cedran yelling about how he wasn't going to help any criminals. That's all I know. Honest."*

Also present is an earlier version of his dialogue about Markarth. His line in the final game, which appears as an ominous warning, was evidently taken from this longer, more literal warning:

:   **What can you tell me about Markarth?**
:   *"Don't fall. [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") the beggar once fell off the crags near the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella"). Legs never healed quite right."*

## Notes

- If Banning has met his end, Cedran may greet you with: *"Poor Banning. Twice as much work here in the stables without him."*

## Bugs

- Banning was supposed to have dinner from 6pm to 7pm, but his work package overrides this.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Baral Sendu

## Overview

| Baral Sendu (RefID: 000E799C) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [The Stumbling Sabrecat](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Stumbling_Sabrecat "Skyrim:The Stumbling Sabrecat") | | |

| Voice Type | [FemaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner") | | |

Baral Sendu

**Baral Sendu** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") found lying dead on his bed in [The Stumbling Sabrecat](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Stumbling_Sabrecat "Skyrim:The Stumbling Sabrecat"), a tavern within [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad"). He was presumably killed by the [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") who have overrun the fort. He wears [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Shoes") and carries a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and up to nine gold.

His body and blood-stained bed are removed during the course of the related quest [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad").

## Bugs

- Baral has the `FemaleCommoner` voice type. This results in a female voice if the body is [resurrected](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, addresses this issue. His voice is set to the `MaleCommoner` voice type.

# Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Bard's Leap Summit ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bard%27s+Leap+Summit)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Lore:Bard's Leap Summit")) | | |

Bard's Leap Summit

**Bard's Leap Summit** is a wooden plank at the very top of [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt").

After fighting your way through a group of Forsworn to get to the top of the ruins, you will see a walkway extending over the edge of a waterfall. If you jump off the walkway into the pool below and survive, a ghost named [Azzadal](/wiki/Skyrim:Azzadal "Skyrim:Azzadal") will appear. He will tell you that he attempted the jump as well, but he obviously failed to survive it. He will then play you a song that will increase your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") by two points. After the initial jump, Azzadal will not appear again and the Speech bonus will not be granted.

When casually jumping off, you might not have enough forward momentum to land in the pool below and avoid the fall damage. Making the jump is possible without tricks, but very good timing is required; you need to hit the jump button at the last possible moment when running toward the ledge. Alternatively, the easiest way is to just sprint off the edge from a sufficient distant instead of jumping off. Surviving the leap is also possible by [becoming ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") before stepping off. The [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") for this is learned at the nearby [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). Another way is to charge off with [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). It is also possible to avoid death by making the jump while mounted. The death of the horse will not matter when using [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").

## Notes

- If you fast travel here, your current horse, if any, will spawn off the side of the plank and fall.
- An [achievement](/wiki/Online:Red_Eagle%27s_Flight "Online:Red Eagle's Flight") can be unlocked by leaping from the same point at [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Online:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Online:Lost Valley Redoubt") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- Sometimes when speaking with Azzadal you can hear him, but there is no sound when he plays his song. You will still receive the Speech bonus.

# Skyrim:Bards College

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Guild Hall: Bards College ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bards+College)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Bards_College "Lore:Bards College")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")* *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SolitudeBardsCollege | |
| Location | |
| [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | |

Exterior of the College

The **Bards College** is a musical school in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The Bards College is where any aspiring bard starts their career in [tale-telling or song](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances"). It is located next door to [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor"), near the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") inside the walls of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The College, though large, contains few notable items. Many of the bards around [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") were trained at the College, and will recommend that the player visit the College. The primary reward for joining the college is actually three of its [miscellaneous quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests"), which together grant +1 to every [skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") (18 points overall). The area contains only one zone, the [interior](#Bards_College).

## Joining the Bards College

Upon arriving at the Bards College, the player is able to seek admittance. It is traditional for new Bards to perform a service to the college before they can be admitted, but there is a problem. The headmaster [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo") will say that no new bards can be admitted except at the festival of the burning of King Olaf, which the bards have held annually, but this year the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") wishes to cancel it as she feels it is in poor taste after the death of [her husband](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg").

Viarmo will ask you to help him reinstate the festival sending you on a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") to retrieve a document lost long ago, an epitaph written at the ancient time of King Olaf's passing, and which he believes will help change the Jarl's mind. The document can be found in [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite"). Once retrieved, return to Viarmo. You must help him fill in the gaps that are rampant in the document. Afterwards, the headmaster takes the player to the Jarl in order to try and reinstate the festival.

## People

## Related Quests

Although there are a handful of quests associated with the Bards College, it does not have a true quest line. For example, there is no [knotwork](/wiki/Skyrim:Quests#Knotwork "Skyrim:Quests") specific to the Bards College, your game statistics do not have a separate category for tracking these quests, and there are no [achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") for entering the college or finishing its quests. The following quests are instead categorized as a [side quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests") and several [miscellaneous quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests"):

### Side Quests

- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the Bards College.

### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Investigate the Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Investigate_the_Bards_College "Skyrim:Investigate the Bards College")**: Investigate the Bards College.
- **[Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute "Skyrim:Finn's Lute")**: Return an invaluable [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").
- **[Pantea's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute")**: Find a missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") for [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia").
- **[Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum")**: Retrieve a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Rjorn.27s_Drum "Skyrim:Quest Items") for [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").

### Other Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Incomplete Quests

- **[Collecting the Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Collecting_the_Edda "Skyrim:Collecting the Edda")**: Collect the parts of the Poetic Edda. ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))

### Exterior

Three [barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel") can be found on the corner of the courtyard across from the entrance. Two [Elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow") and a [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing") can be found on the balcony.

### Ground Floor (Library and Trainer's Bedrooms)

The building itself has two entrances, the main entrance via the courtyard and the rear entrance that enters into the basement near the kitchen and student's quarters. There are a large number of books and musical instruments throughout the building and most of the crockery is of high quality.

Entry from the courtyard brings you into a reception area with a wooden bench against the northeast wall; in front of this is a low table holding a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), while against the southwest wall is a set of shelves and a small unit with a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") on a shelf and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") in a pot. To the southeast is a stairwell with stairs leading up to the top floor to the practice and lecture rooms and down to the basement to the kitchen and student's quarters. There is a red mountain flower on the end of the banister, in a pot, behind a large plant. On this floor the library is to the southwest and the teacher's bedrooms are to the northeast.

The library contains many common books on various bookcases, with tables and chairs arranged around the room. Some of the less common books found in the library include *[Feyfolken II](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_II "Skyrim:Feyfolken II")*, *[The Wild Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wild_Elves "Skyrim:The Wild Elves")*, *[N'Gasta! Kvata! Kvakis!](/wiki/Skyrim:N%27Gasta!_Kvata!_Kvakis! "Skyrim:N'Gasta! Kvata! Kvakis!")*, *[On Stepping Lightly](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Stepping_Lightly "Skyrim:On Stepping Lightly")* and *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*, which if you haven't read a copy previously will initiate a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages") to investigate [Arkngthamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Arkngthamz "Skyrim:Arkngthamz"), a Dwemer ruin located in [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). There is also a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* which will initiate a misc quest to [find red eagle's sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)"). After starting [a quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts") for [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") to find a rare book, a copy of it, the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")* can be found on the counter in the library. On top of two of the bookcases against the southeast wall are a random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") while against the northeast wall is a small unit holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine").

To the northeast of the reception area is an internal wall with a small cupboard against it, following the corridor to the northwest, past two more cupboard, one on either side of the corridor, the first has a bunch of lavender on a shelf above it. The door at the end of the corridor leads into the bedroom belonging to [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo"), which contains a double four-poster bed coming out from the northwest wall with an end table on either side and a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items at the foot of the bed. Against the southwest wall is an open crate, behind the door containing a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a bunch of lavender, further to the right is a narrow wooden table with a platter holding two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a couple of pieces of cheese and a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") of red and green apples. Against the northeast wall is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and with a bunch of lavender on top. There is a washbasin to the right and a narrow wooden table beside that. In the eastern corner of the room is a dressing area with a cupboard against the northeast wall, with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top and a wall shelf holding an unlocked chest containing leveled items above it. Opposite this against the southwest wall are two tall wardrobe containing a mixture of fine clothes and clutter. On the corner of this wall, beside the door, is a large vase containing another bunch of lavender.

From the previous corridor there is another bedroom to the northeast belonging to [Pantea Ateia](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia") with a narrow wooden table outside against the northwest wall. This room contains a double bed coming out from the northwest wall with a small wardrobe on either side and a washbasin to the right in front of a basket containing a small coin purse. Against the southwest wall is a narrow wooden table with a bowl of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a plate holding a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a bunch of lavender on top. Above this is a wall shelf holding a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") and a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower. Against the northeast wall is a narrow wooden table and a bookcase containing eight common books and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") with another book on the floor in front of it, while against the southeast wall is a wooden table with a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on top, with a tall vase and wooden bench to the right of it.

The next bedroom along to the southeast belongs to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers"). It contains a large single bed coming out from the northeast wall with an end table to the right. Against the southeast wall are two wall shelves holding a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing") and a bunch of lavender. To the right of these is a narrow wooden table, while against the southwest wall is a wooden bench and corner shelf that holds a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"). Against the northwest wall are two pairs of bookcases separated by two more coming out from the wall. There bookcases hold a total of thirty-nine common books, including a copy of *[Walking the World, Vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")*, which will update your map if you haven't discovered all of the places mentioned in and around [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). There are also two less common books, *[Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge_Letters,_v1 "Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1")* and *[Invocation of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Invocation_of_Azura "Skyrim:Invocation of Azura")*, a [potion of extreme magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Magicka"), a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina") and a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"). There is a low table and chair on the northern corner of the room with a single common book on top.

The last bedroom on this floor belongs to [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane") and is next door to the southeast of Inge Six Fingers' bedroom. It contains a single bed coming out diagonally from the southern corner with an end table to the right and an open crate at the foot of the bed. Against the southeast wall is a small wardrobe containing fine clothes and with a [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"), a common book and a bunch of tundra cotton on top. Against the northeast wall is a wooden bench, while against the northwest wall are two wall shelves, both with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), above a narrow wooden table. To the right are two sets of shelves holding a collection of flutes, drums, a lute and three common books. In front of these is a low table and chair with a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and a bunch of lavender on top of the table and another drum on the floor in the northern corner. Outside Giraud's bedroom is a low table and chair with a bunch of lavender and a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") on top of the table.

### Top Floor (Lecture/Practice Rooms)

At the top of the stairs there is a small cupboard on the left with a red mountain flower in a pot on top. Opposite the stairs in a small balcony that overlooks the reception area with a large planter holding two deathbell plants and an open crate containing ten common books. There is a second cupboard next to a wooden bench at the rear of the balcony, over the stairs. The corridor leads to rooms at the northeast and southwest ends of the building.

To the northeast there is a cupboard against the southeast wall with an open crate containing three more common books, opposite a small storeroom, which contains a small cupboard against the northwest wall and two sets of shelves against the northeast wall. These hold two [quicksilver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ingot "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ingot"), while opposite against the southwest wall are a stack of crates and a couple of rugs. The main lecture and practice room has a lectern on a raised dais at the northeastern end of the room over looking three wooden benches facing it. In the northern corner of the room is a planter containing a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plant, with a potion of health hidden among the leaves. Against the southwest wall are two wall shelves holding three common books, while against the northeast wall are two more wooden benches, with two more against the southeast wall separated by two pairs of bookcases back-to-back coming out from the middle of the southeast wall holding a total of thirty common books, including *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")* which adds map markers for [The Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones"), [The Lover Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover_Stone "Skyrim:The Lover Stone"), [The Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") and [The Shadow Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shadow_Stone "Skyrim:The Shadow Stone"). Some of the less common books on these shelves include a copy of *[The Pig Children](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pig_Children "Skyrim:The Pig Children")*, *[The Seed](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Seed "Skyrim:The Seed")*, *[Feyfolken I](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_I "Skyrim:Feyfolken I")*, a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")* and a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* which, if you haven't already initiated the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend") will add a map marker and direct you to [Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur"). There is also a low table in the eastern corner of the room with three common books on top. Against the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health").

To the southwest in the corridor there are two small cupboards against the southeast wall, opposite two narrow wooden tables with three common books, a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a bowl containing a sprig of snowberries on top. The main lecture and practice room at the end of the corridor has a lectern on a raised dais facing three wooden benches that have several drums and flute on them, to the southeast. There is a planter containing a deathbell plant in the northern corner, next to a narrow wooden table which has a sprig of snowberries on top against the northeast wall. At the rear of the room there is a set of shelves coming out from the southeast wall holding a couple of drums, a flute and a lute, with a planter containing two deathbell plants to the left and a wooden bench to the right. In the eastern corner there is a basket containing a potion of minor stamina, with a small cupboard to the left, against the northeast wall with a lute on top. Opposite this is a wooden bench against the southwest wall and a low table in front, with a bunch of tundra cotton, a sprig of snowberries and a flute on top.

### Basement (Kitchen and Student's Quarters)

Descending the stairs leads to an open area with two clusters of seating arranged around low tables and two small cupboards, one against the northeast wall and the other against the southwest wall. To the southwest is a large opening into the kitchen where [Bendt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bendt "Skyrim:Bendt") spends his days. It contains four long wooden tables, one against the against the southeast wall has a baked potato and two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on top. One against the northwest wall has a bottle of alto wine and two more salmon steaks on top and a rack hanging above from the wall holding a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). The third is in the middle of the room between the other two and has a baked potato, two salmon steaks, two loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a platter holding another two baked potatoes, a sweet roll and two pieces of goat cheese. These three all have benches beside them.

The fourth table appears to be used for preparing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and is in front of the oven on the southwest wall. There is another baked potato and an empty pot in the oven, while on the table there are a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two bulbs of garlic, three fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). In the eastern corner is a large round table and chair with a plate of bread and cheese on the table. Against the northwest wall is a small unit holding a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") and a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), while in the southern corner are two sets of shelves holding four red apples, a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a salmon steak, a fillet of salmon meat, a [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), five garlic bulbs, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two loaves of bread, a potato and several pieces of cheese. To the right of the oven is a rack hanging from the southwest wall with two cooked [horse haunches](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch") and a raw haunch of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") above a wood pile and block with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against it.

To the right of these is a doorway to Bendt's L-shaped bedroom which contains a tall wardrobe against the southwest wall, with a dresser to the right that has a plate of bread and cheese on top. There is a single bed in the northern corner with a small low table beside it which has a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* on top and against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding a bottle of alto wine, a [chef's tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Chef's Tunic") and [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat"), and a woodcutter's axe.

To the northeast is an area with several food sacks on the floor, while around the corner to the southeast there is a stack of crates and a small cupboard flanking the rear entrance. To the northwest is the student's quarters with a row of four single beds all coming out from the southwest wall, with a small table beside each of them and partitions separating each of them. The small tables have either a common book or small item of food on each. Against the northeast wall there are two tall wardrobes containing fine clothes, with a dresser at either end containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes").

## Notes

- For a complete list of the various Bard performances, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances").
- Even after being admitted into the college, the beds are not open for you to rest in, neither will you ever rise in ranks or take any active part in College business.
- Other than most barrels and sacks, all containers in the Bards College are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- For the three quests involving the retrieval of instruments, the script for removal of the quest items from one's inventory at the completion of the quest is bugged. As such, these items will permanently be in your inventory (they're flagged as Quest items). Owners of the PC version of Skyrim can use console commands to remove these items from their inventory.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes the objective "Investigate the Bards College" cannot be completed. Starting this quest after you have already joined the Bards College will make this quest incompletable, permanently leaving this task in your quest journal. The quest indicator points at the quest target but no dialogue options are present. You can clear the "Investigate the Bards College" quest by typing `SetObjectiveCompleted MS05Start 10 1` into the console.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- All class sessions can be started even if none of the students are present. The instructional lines from each teacher have a tendency to play from wherever they happen to be in the building.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- If your first visit to the Bards College doesn't take place until after King Olaf's Verse has been recovered, the pointer quest to investigate the College may fail to terminate.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- After completing Battle for Solitude, the Imperial banners don't change for the Stormcloak ones. **?**
